The [`python/triton/language`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language) directory defines data types (e.g., [`int1`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L807), [`float16`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L821)), tensor operations (e.g., [`load`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1424), [`store`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1164), [`dot`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L2266)), mathematical functions (e.g., [`exp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1194), [`log`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1197)), atomic operations (e.g., [`atomic_add`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1176)), and control flow primitives (e.g., [`arange`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1892), [`program_id`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1856)). The [`TritonSemantic`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/semantic.py#L26) class in [`python/triton/language/semantic.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/semantic.py) handles the creation of IR instructions, type checking, and the application of semantic rules during AST to IR conversion. These language constructs allow users to precisely control GPU computations, from memory access patterns to parallel execution strategies.  
Python 前端还暴露了核心的 Triton 语言特性和语义规则。 `python/triton/language` 目录定义了数据类型（例如 `int1` 、 `float16` ）、张量操作（例如 `load` 、 `store` 、 `dot` ）、数学函数（例如 `exp` 、 `log` ）、原子操作（例如 `atomic_add` ）以及控制流原语（例如 `arange` 、 `program_id` ）。 `python/triton/language/semantic.py` 中的 `TritonSemantic` 类负责处理 IR 指令的创建、类型检查以及在 AST 到 IR 转换过程中应用语义规则。这些语言结构允许用户精确控制 GPU 计算，从内存访问模式到并行执行策略。

For advanced users and specific hardware targets, Triton offers an experimental Gluon frontend, primarily located in [`python/triton/experimental/gluon`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon). This frontend provides lower-level control for architectures like NVIDIA Hopper and Blackwell, featuring specialized IR dialects, custom memory layouts, and fine-grained operations such as Tensor Memory Accelerator (TMA) and Warp-Group Matrix Multiply-Accumulate (WMMA). Examples in [`python/examples/gluon`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon) demonstrate its use for highly optimized deep learning kernels.  
对于高级用户和特定的硬件目标，Triton 提供了一个实验性的 Gluon 前端，主要位于 `python/triton/experimental/gluon` 。这个前端为 NVIDIA Hopper 和 Blackwell 等架构提供了较低级别的控制，具有专门的中间表示方言、自定义内存布局以及细粒度的操作，例如 Tensor Memory Accelerator（TMA）和 Warp-Group Matrix Multiply-Accumulate（WMMA）。 `python/examples/gluon` 中的示例展示了它用于高度优化的深度学习内核的使用方法。

Finally, the runtime environment in [`python/triton/runtime`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime) manages memory allocation ([`python/triton/runtime/_allocation.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/_allocation.py)), selects the appropriate GPU driver ([`python/triton/runtime/driver.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/driver.py)), and provides an interpreter ([`python/triton/runtime/interpreter.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/interpreter.py)) for debugging kernels on the CPU without requiring GPU hardware. The [`python/triton/knobs.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/knobs.py) module allows for comprehensive runtime configuration, enabling users to adjust compilation, caching, and execution parameters through environment variables or Python APIs.  
最后， `python/triton/runtime` 中的运行时环境管理内存分配（ `python/triton/runtime/_allocation.py` ）、选择合适的 GPU 驱动（ `python/triton/runtime/driver.py` ），并提供一个解释器（ `python/triton/runtime/interpreter.py` ），用于在 CPU 上调试内核，而无需 GPU 硬件。 `python/triton/knobs.py` 模块允许进行全面的运行时配置，使用户能够通过环境变量或 Python API 调整编译、缓存和执行参数。

### Python AST to Triton IR Conversion  
Python AST 到 Triton IR 转换

link

zoom\_in

The process of converting Python Abstract Syntax Trees (ASTs) of Triton kernels into Triton's internal intermediate representation (IR) is managed by the directory [`python/triton/compiler`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler). This conversion is a foundational step in compiling Triton kernels for GPU execution.  
将 Triton 内核的 Python 抽象语法树（ASTs）转换为 Triton 的内部中间表示（IR）的过程由目录 `python/triton/compiler` 管理。这一转换是编译 Triton 内核以在 GPU 上执行的基础步骤。

The primary component responsible for this translation is the [`CodeGenerator`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/code_generator.py#L274) class, found in [`python/triton/compiler/code_generator.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/code_generator.py). This class traverses the Python AST of a JIT-compiled Triton function, transforming Python language constructs into corresponding IR operations. During this traversal, the [`CodeGenerator`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/code_generator.py#L274) handles several key aspects:  
负责此次翻译的主要组件是 `CodeGenerator` 类，位于 `python/triton/compiler/code_generator.py` 中。该类遍历 JIT 编译的 Triton 函数的 Python 抽象语法树（AST），将 Python 语言结构转换为相应的中间表示（IR）操作。在此遍历过程中， `CodeGenerator` 处理了几个关键方面：

-   **Scope Management:** It maintains global and local scopes ([`gscope`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/code_generator.py#L134) and [`lscope`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/code_generator.py#L117)) to ensure correct variable resolution and type inference, differentiating between standard variables and [`constexpr`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L209) values.  
    作用域管理：它维护全局和局部作用域（ `gscope` 和 `lscope` ）以确保正确的变量解析和类型推断，区分标准变量和 `constexpr` 值。
-   **IR Generation:** An IR builder ([`ir.builder`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L149) or [`gluon_ir.GluonOpBuilder`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/code_generator.py#L283)) is used to emit MLIR operations. This includes creating operations for basic constants, types, arithmetic, logical operations, and memory access patterns. Triton-specific operations, such as [`create_get_program_id`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/interpreter.py#L406) and [`create_dot`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/interpreter.py#L605), are also generated at this stage, using the bindings provided in [`python/src/ir.cc`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/ir.cc) and [`python/src/gluon_ir.cc`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/gluon_ir.cc).  
    中间表示生成：使用中间表示构建器（ `ir.builder` 或 `gluon_ir.GluonOpBuilder` ）来生成 MLIR 操作。这包括为基本常量、类型、算术、逻辑操作和内存访问模式创建操作。在此时还会生成特定于 Triton 的操作，如 `create_get_program_id` 和 `create_dot` ，使用在 `python/src/ir.cc` 和 `python/src/gluon_ir.cc` 中提供的绑定。
-   **Type Inference and Propagation:** The system infers and propagates data types throughout the AST, converting Python types into Triton's internal [`base_type`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L159) and [`ir.type`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L177) representations. This is crucial for ensuring type compatibility and correctness in the generated IR.  
    类型推断与传播：系统在整个抽象语法树（AST）中推断和传播数据类型，将 Python 类型转换为 Triton 的内部 `base_type` 和 `ir.type` 表示。这对于确保生成的中间表示（IR）的类型兼容性和正确性至关重要。
-   **Control Flow Translation:** Python control flow constructs like [`if`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/setup.py#L44), [`while`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/README.md?plain=1#L101), and [`for`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/LICENSE#L18) statements are translated into MLIR equivalents. This involves managing loop-carried variables and conditional branching logic, often utilizing [`scf.if`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/Proton/scope_id.mlir#L140) or [`scf.for`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/Triton/vecadd.mlir#L21) operations for structured control flow.  
    控制流翻译：Python 控制流结构如 `if` 、 `while` 和 `for` 语句被翻译成 MLIR 等价物。这涉及管理循环变量和条件分支逻辑，通常使用 `scf.if` 或 `scf.for` 操作来处理结构化控制流。
-   **Function Call Handling:** Calls to other JIT-compiled functions, built-ins, and [`constexpr`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L209) functions are managed, including argument mangling to ensure unique function names for different argument types, supporting function overloading and specialization.  
    函数调用处理：对其他 JIT 编译的函数、内置函数和 `constexpr` 函数的调用被管理，包括参数修饰以确保不同参数类型具有唯一函数名，支持函数重载和特化。
-   **Constant Evaluation:** [`constexpr`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L209) values are identified and evaluated at compile time when possible, enabling static optimizations before code generation.  
    常量求值： `constexpr` 值在可能的情况下在编译时被识别和求值，使得在代码生成之前可以进行静态优化。

The entry point for this conversion is typically the [`ast_to_ttir`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/code_generator.py#L1620) function in [`python/triton/compiler/code_generator.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/code_generator.py). This function initializes the [`CodeGenerator`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/code_generator.py#L274) and begins the AST traversal, setting up initial argument types based on the function's signature and [`constexpr`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L209) constants.  
这个转换的入口通常是 `python/triton/compiler/code_generator.py` 中的 `ast_to_ttir` 函数。该函数初始化 `CodeGenerator` 并开始 AST 遍历，根据函数的签名和 `constexpr` 常量设置初始参数类型。

The [`TritonOpBuilder`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/ir.h#L7) class, defined in [`python/src/ir.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/ir.h), facilitates the creation of MLIR operations by automatically managing source location tracking, which is valuable for debugging and error reporting. The [`PassManager`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/ir.cc#L23) class, also exposed through [`python/src/ir.cc`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/ir.cc), enables the application of various MLIR passes for transformation and optimization of the generated IR. Error handling during this process is managed through a custom exception hierarchy, defined in [`python/triton/compiler/errors.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/errors.py), which provides detailed error messages including source code context. The overall orchestration of the compilation pipeline, including cache management and stage progression, is handled by the [`compile`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/compiler.py#L226) function in [`python/triton/compiler/compiler.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/compiler.py). See [JIT Compilation, Caching, and Kernel Execution](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#python-frontend-and-jit-compilation-jit-compilation-caching-and-kernel-execution) for more details.  
`TritonOpBuilder` 类，定义在 `python/src/ir.h` 中，通过自动管理源位置跟踪，简化了 MLIR 操作的创建，这对调试和错误报告非常有价值。 `PassManager` 类，也通过 `python/src/ir.cc` 暴露，能够应用各种 MLIR 遍历，用于生成 IR 的转换和优化。此过程中的错误处理通过在 `python/triton/compiler/errors.py` 中定义的自定义异常层次结构进行管理，该结构提供详细的错误消息，包括源代码上下文。编译流程的整体协调，包括缓存管理和阶段进展，由 `python/triton/compiler/compiler.py` 中的 `compile` 函数处理。更多详情请参阅 JIT 编译、缓存和内核执行。

### Triton Language Features and Semantic Rules  
Triton 语言特性和语义规则

link

zoom\_in

The Triton language provides core programming constructs and data types for defining GPU kernels, focusing on high-performance mathematical, tensor, and atomic operations. The [`python/triton/language`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language) directory centralizes these features, making them accessible for Triton-native programming.  
Triton 语言提供了用于定义 GPU 内核的核心编程结构和数据类型，专注于高性能的数学、张量和原子操作。 `python/triton/language` 目录集中了这些特性，使其可用于 Triton 原生编程。

At its foundation, Triton employs a system of data types and tensor representations defined primarily in [`python/triton/language/core.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py). This includes primitive types such as integers ([`int32`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L810), [`int64`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L811), [`uint8`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L812)), various floating-point types ([`float16`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L821), [`bfloat16`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L822), [`float32`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L823), [`float64`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L824), and specialized [`float8`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/_internal_testing.py#L139) formats), as well as [`pointer_type`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L666), [`block_type`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L706), and [`tensor_descriptor_type`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1484) for advanced memory access patterns. Compile-time constants are represented by [`constexpr`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L209), allowing expressions involving these values to be evaluated during compilation for optimization. The [`tensor`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L857) object serves as the fundamental N-dimensional array structure, overloading standard Python operators for arithmetic, bitwise, and comparison operations.  
在其基础上，Triton 采用了一套数据类型和张量表示系统，这些系统主要在 `python/triton/language/core.py` 中定义。这包括诸如整数（ `int32` , `int64` , `uint8` ）、各种浮点类型（ `float16` , `bfloat16` , `float32` , `float64` 以及特殊的 `float8` 格式），以及用于高级内存访问模式的 `pointer_type` , `block_type` , 和 `tensor_descriptor_type` 。编译时常量由 `constexpr` 表示，允许在编译期间对这些值进行表达式求值以进行优化。 `tensor` 对象作为基本的 N 维数组结构，重载了标准 Python 运算符以进行算术、位运算和比较操作。

The semantic rules and how these operations translate into the intermediate representation (IR) are managed by the [`TritonSemantic`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/semantic.py#L26) class within [`python/triton/language/semantic.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/semantic.py). This class acts as an interface to the IR builder, handling crucial aspects like type checking, implicit type casting, and broadcasting for binary operations. It ensures that operations adhere to Triton's type system, which includes C-like integer promotion rules and specific handling for floating-point precision and pointer arithmetic. The [`TritonSemantic`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/semantic.py#L26) class also governs the creation of IR instructions for functions that provide metadata for compilation, such as [`program_id`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1856) and [`num_programs`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1875), which return the current program instance ID and the total number of programs along a specified axis, respectively.  
语义规则以及这些操作如何转换为中间表示（IR）由 `TritonSemantic` 类在 `python/triton/language/semantic.py` 中管理。该类充当 IR 构建器的接口，处理类型检查、隐式类型转换和二元操作的广播等关键方面。它确保操作符合 Triton 的类型系统，该系统包括类似 C 的整数提升规则，以及针对浮点精度和指针算术的特定处理。 `TritonSemantic` 类还负责为提供编译元数据的函数创建 IR 指令，例如 `program_id` 和 `num_programs` ，分别返回当前程序实例 ID 和沿指定轴的程序总数。

Mathematical functions, defined in [`python/triton/language/math.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/math.py), include common unary operations like [`exp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1194), [`log`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1197), [`cos`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1200), [`sin`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1203), [`sqrt`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1206), [`abs`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1212), and [`erf`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/math.py#L217), as well as binary operations like [`fdiv`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/math.py#L196) and [`fma`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/math.py#L242). These functions feature robust data type checking using decorators like [`_check_dtype`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/math.py#L8) to ensure compatibility with GPU accelerators and to guide users towards supported data types. The underlying IR instruction creation is handled by the [`_semantic`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/jit.py#L1127) layer, which translates these high-level operations into efficient low-level IR.  
数学函数，定义在 `python/triton/language/math.py` 中，包括常见的单目运算如 `exp` 、 `log` 、 `cos` 、 `sin` 、 `sqrt` 、 `abs` 和 `erf` ，以及双目运算如 `fdiv` 和 `fma` 。这些函数通过使用 `_check_dtype` 等装饰器进行健壮的数据类型检查，以确保与 GPU 加速器的兼容性，并引导用户使用支持的数据类型。底层的 IR 指令创建由 `_semantic` 层处理，将这些高级操作转换为高效的低级 IR。

Tensor manipulation functions are available through [`python/triton/language/standard.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/standard.py). This includes operations such as [`reshape`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1155), [`squeeze`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/standard.py#L563), [`unsqueeze`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/standard.py#L569), [`broadcast`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1946), [`cat`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L2036), and [`permute`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1146). More complex operations like [`max`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1239), [`min`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1245), [`sum`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1251), [`argmax`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1242), [`argmin`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1248), and [`sort`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1266) are also provided, often incorporating type promotion logic to prevent overflow or precision loss during reductions and ensure numerical stability. Sorting algorithms, for instance, utilize bitonic sort-like implementations for parallel execution on GPUs.  
通过 `python/triton/language/standard.py` 可以使用张量操作函数。这包括 `reshape` 、 `squeeze` 、 `unsqueeze` 、 `broadcast` 、 `cat` 和 `permute` 等操作。还提供了更复杂的操作，如 `max` 、 `min` 、 `sum` 、 `argmax` 、 `argmin` 和 `sort` ，这些操作通常包含类型提升逻辑，以防止在归约过程中发生溢出或精度损失，并确保数值稳定性。例如，排序算法会使用类似位 onic 排序的实现，以便在 GPU 上并行执行。

Memory operations are a core component of the Triton language, including [`load`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1424) and [`store`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1164) for reading and writing data, respectively, to arbitrary memory addresses. These operations support masking, boundary checks, and cache/eviction policies. For fine-grained control and advanced memory access patterns, [`tensor_descriptor_type`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1484) in [`python/triton/language/core.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py) and its associated operations in [`python/triton/language/semantic.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/semantic.py) are used, especially for hardware-accelerated memory transfers. Triton also supports atomic operations like [`atomic_add`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1176), [`atomic_max`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1179), and [`atomic_cas`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1170), enabling safe concurrent access to shared memory locations within kernels. These atomic operations also involve type and pointer checks to ensure correctness.  
内存操作是 Triton 语言的核心组成部分，包括 `load` 和 `store` 分别用于从任意内存地址读取和写入数据。这些操作支持掩码、边界检查和缓存/驱逐策略。对于细粒度控制和高级内存访问模式，使用 `tensor_descriptor_type` 中的 `python/triton/language/core.py` 及其在 `python/triton/language/semantic.py` 中的相关操作，特别是用于硬件加速的内存传输。Triton 还支持 `atomic_add` 、 `atomic_max` 和 `atomic_cas` 等原子操作，能够在内核中安全地并发访问共享内存位置。这些原子操作还涉及类型和指针检查，以确保正确性。

Random number generation, implemented in [`python/triton/language/random.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/random.py), utilizes the Philox algorithm to produce pseudo-random numbers. Functions like [`randint`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/random.py#L73) and [`rand`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/random.py#L147) generate uniform integers and floats, while [`randn`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/random.py#L191) generates normally distributed floats, often using techniques like the Box-Muller transform. These functions are designed to leverage Just-In-Time (JIT) compilation for performance.  
随机数生成，在 `python/triton/language/random.py` 中实现，利用 Philox 算法生成伪随机数。函数 `randint` 和 `rand` 生成均匀分布的整数和浮点数，而 `randn` 生成正态分布的浮点数，通常使用 Box-Muller 变换等技术。这些函数设计为利用即时编译（JIT）来提升性能。

Triton's design also incorporates mechanisms to adapt to different hardware targets. The [`target_info`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/__init__.py#L139) module in [`python/triton/language/target_info.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/target_info.py) provides utilities to query backend information (e.g., CUDA or HIP) and compute capabilities. Functions decorated with [`@constexpr_function`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/__init__.py#L67) allow for compile-time branching and optimization based on the target hardware, enabling the generation of efficient kernels across various GPU architectures.  
Triton 的设计还包含了适应不同硬件目标的机制。在 `python/triton/language/target_info.py` 中的 `target_info` 模块提供了查询后端信息（例如 CUDA 或 HIP）和计算能力的工具。使用 `@constexpr_function` 装饰的函数允许在编译时根据目标硬件进行分支和优化，从而能够在各种 GPU 架构上生成高效的内核。

Overall, the Triton language features provide a comprehensive set of tools for writing high-performance GPU kernels, with strong emphasis on type safety, semantic correctness, and optimization for diverse hardware. The integration with Triton's compiler infrastructure, described in [Triton Compiler Architecture](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#triton-compiler-architecture), ensures that these language constructs are efficiently translated into machine-specific code.  
总体而言，Triton 语言特性提供了一套全面的工具，用于编写高性能 GPU 内核，并高度重视类型安全、语义正确性以及对多种硬件的优化。与 Triton 编译器架构中描述的编译器基础设施的集成，确保这些语言结构能够高效地转换为特定于机器的代码。

### JIT Compilation, Caching, and Kernel Execution  
JIT 编译、缓存和内核执行

link

zoom\_in

The Just-In-Time (JIT) compilation lifecycle in Triton begins with the [`jit`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/jit.py#L913) decorator in [`python/triton/runtime/jit.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/jit.py), which marks a Python function for compilation into a high-performance Triton kernel. This decorator transforms the decorated function into a [`JITFunction`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/jit.py#L620) instance, which serves as the core representation of a JIT-compiled kernel.  
Triton 中的 Just-In-Time（JIT）编译生命周期从 `jit` 中的 `python/triton/runtime/jit.py` 装饰器开始，该装饰器用于标记 Python 函数，将其编译为高性能的 Triton 内核。此装饰器将装饰的函数转换为 `JITFunction` 实例，该实例作为 JIT 编译内核的核心表示。

The [`JITFunction`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/jit.py#L620) manages the entire compilation and execution process. When a [`JITFunction`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/jit.py#L620) is invoked, it first handles argument parsing and kernel specialization based on the input types and values. This specialization process tailors the kernel for optimal performance on the target hardware given specific inputs. To avoid redundant compilation, Triton employs a robust caching mechanism. A unique cache key is generated for each kernel based on its source code, dependencies, and compilation parameters, ensuring that already compiled kernels can be quickly retrieved. This caching is managed by [`CacheManager`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/cache.py#L14) implementations, such as [`FileCacheManager`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/cache.py#L36) for local storage and [`RemoteCacheManager`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/cache.py#L168) (using backends like [`RedisRemoteCacheBackend`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/cache.py#L146)) for remote caching, as defined in [`python/triton/runtime/cache.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/cache.py).  
`JITFunction` 管理整个编译和执行过程。当调用 `JITFunction` 时，它首先处理参数解析和基于输入类型和值的内核专有化。这种专有化过程针对特定输入，在目标硬件上优化内核性能。为了避免重复编译，Triton 采用了一个强大的缓存机制。每个内核根据其源代码、依赖项和编译参数生成一个唯一的缓存键，确保已经编译的内核可以快速检索。这种缓存由 `CacheManager` 实现，例如 `FileCacheManager` 用于本地存储和 `RemoteCacheManager` （使用 `RedisRemoteCacheBackend` 等后端）用于远程缓存，如 `python/triton/runtime/cache.py` 中定义的那样。

The actual compilation process is orchestrated by the [`_do_compile`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/jit.py#L869) method within [`JITFunction`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/jit.py#L620). This method can leverage asynchronous compilation, as implemented in [`python/triton/runtime/_async_compile.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/_async_compile.py), allowing compilation tasks to run in the background without blocking the main execution thread. The [`AsyncCompileMode`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/_async_compile.py#L37) context manager handles the submission and finalization of these asynchronous tasks. Once compiled, the [`CompiledKernel`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/compiler.py#L407) object, described in [Python AST to Triton IR Conversion](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#python-frontend-and-jit-compilation-python-ast-to-triton-ir-conversion), contains the GPU binary and metadata, ready for execution.  
实际的编译过程由 `JITFunction` 中的 `_do_compile` 方法协调。该方法可以利用 `python/triton/runtime/_async_compile.py` 中实现的异步编译，允许编译任务在后台运行而不会阻塞主执行线程。 `AsyncCompileMode` 上下文管理器负责提交和最终化这些异步任务。一旦编译完成，根据 Python AST 到 Triton IR 转换中描述的 `CompiledKernel` 对象，包含 GPU 二进制和元数据，准备执行。

For kernel execution, [`JITFunction`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/jit.py#L620)'s [`run`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/setup.py#L200) method orchestrates the launch of the compiled kernel on the GPU. This involves loading the binary into the GPU driver and setting up a launcher function. Triton also includes sophisticated memory allocation management, with the [`python/triton/runtime/_allocation.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/_allocation.py) module providing interfaces for pluggable [`Allocator`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/_allocation.py#L11) strategies. This allows kernels to request additional global memory workspaces dynamically, supporting various memory management approaches. Runtime errors, such as [`OutOfResources`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/errors.py#L14) or [`PTXASError`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/errors.py#L29), are handled by specific exception classes defined in [`python/triton/runtime/errors.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/errors.py). In addition to GPU execution, an interpreter, detailed in [`python/triton/runtime/interpreter.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/interpreter.py), allows Triton kernels to be executed on the CPU, primarily for debugging purposes. This interpreter dynamically patches Triton language constructs to simulate kernel behavior using NumPy.  
对于内核执行， `JITFunction` 的 `run` 方法负责在 GPU 上启动编译好的内核。这包括将二进制文件加载到 GPU 驱动程序中，并设置一个启动函数。Triton 还包括复杂的内存分配管理，其中 `python/triton/runtime/_allocation.py` 模块提供了可插拔的 `Allocator` 策略的接口。这使得内核能够动态请求额外的全局内存工作区，支持多种内存管理方法。运行时错误，如 `OutOfResources` 或 `PTXASError` ，由 `python/triton/runtime/errors.py` 中定义的特定异常类处理。除了 GPU 执行外，一个解释器（详细说明见 `python/triton/runtime/interpreter.py` ）允许 Triton 内核在 CPU 上执行，主要用于调试目的。这个解释器动态地修补 Triton 语言结构，使用 NumPy 模拟内核行为。

### Autotuning and Performance Heuristics  
自动调优和性能启发式方法

link

zoom\_in

Triton includes capabilities for automatically optimizing the performance of kernels through autotuning and heuristic-based parameter selection. This allows Triton to benchmark different kernel configurations and dynamically adapt parameters to achieve optimal performance for specific hardware and input data.  
Triton 包含通过自动调优和基于启发式的参数选择来自动优化内核性能的功能。这使得 Triton 能够对不同的内核配置进行基准测试，并动态调整参数以针对特定的硬件和输入数据实现最佳性能。

The [`autotune`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py#L380) decorator, defined in [`python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py), enables this process by wrapping a Just-In-Time (JIT) compiled kernel. An [`Autotuner`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py#L19) instance benchmarks various [`Config`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py#L300) objects—which define kernel parameters such as [`num_warps`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/knobs.py#L437), [`num_stages`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/knobs.py#L439), and meta-parameters ([`kwargs`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/docs/conf.py#L110))—to identify the configuration that yields the best performance for a given set of input arguments. The [`Autotuner`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py#L19) uses caching mechanisms, both in-memory and disk-based, to store and retrieve previously benchmarked results, avoiding redundant computations for frequently called kernels with the same input characteristics. To manage the state of kernel arguments during benchmarking, the [`Autotuner`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py#L19) supports optional [`pre_hook`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py#L21) and [`post_hook`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py#L21) functions. Furthermore, to accelerate the tuning process, particularly for kernels with a large number of possible configurations, the [`Autotuner`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py#L19) incorporates configuration pruning strategies, which can involve early filtering of configurations or leveraging performance models to select promising candidates.  
`autotune` 装饰器，定义在 `python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py` 中，通过包装即时编译（JIT）的内核来启用此过程。 `Autotuner` 实例对各种 `Config` 对象进行基准测试——这些对象定义了内核参数，如 `num_warps` 、 `num_stages` 和元参数（ `kwargs` ），以识别在给定输入参数集上表现最佳的配置。 `Autotuner` 使用内存和基于磁盘的缓存机制来存储和检索先前基准测试的结果，避免对具有相同输入特征的频繁调用内核进行重复计算。为了在基准测试期间管理内核参数的状态， `Autotuner` 支持可选的 `pre_hook` 和 `post_hook` 函数。此外，为了加速调优过程，特别是对于具有大量可能配置的内核， `Autotuner` 结合了配置剪枝策略，这可能涉及早期过滤配置或利用性能模型来选择有希望的候选者。

Alternatively, the [`heuristics`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py#L449) decorator, also defined in [`python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py), provides a mechanism for dynamic parameter computation without exhaustive benchmarking. This approach is suitable when performance characteristics can be predicted based on input properties or hardware specifics. The [`Heuristics`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py#L449) class stores a mapping of meta-parameter names to heuristic functions. When the kernel is executed, these functions are invoked with the kernel's arguments to dynamically compute the optimal values for the meta-parameters, which are then used to configure the kernel for execution.  
或者， `heuristics` 装饰器（同样定义在 `python/triton/runtime/autotuner.py` 中）提供了一种无需穷举基准测试的动态参数计算机制。当性能特征可以根据输入属性或硬件特定信息预测时，这种方法是合适的。 `Heuristics` 类存储了元参数名称到启发式函数的映射。当内核被执行时，这些函数会被用内核的参数调用，以动态计算元参数的最佳值，然后这些值用于配置内核以执行。

These autotuning and heuristic capabilities are seamlessly integrated with Triton's JIT compilation and kernel execution pipeline, as described in [JIT Compilation, Caching, and Kernel Execution](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#python-frontend-and-jit-compilation-jit-compilation-caching-and-kernel-execution). The [`JITFunction`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/jit.py#L620) class, located in [`python/triton/runtime/jit.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/jit.py), plays a central role by handling argument parsing, specialization, and the eventual launch of the optimized kernel. The runtime environment, managed by the [`driver`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Dialect/Triton/Transforms/LoopAwareCSE.cpp#L94) in [`python/triton/runtime/driver.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/driver.py), ensures that the selected configurations are applied to the appropriate backend for execution. Caching of compiled artifacts, including tuning results, is handled by the [`cache`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/include/triton/Dialect/TritonGPU/IR/Dialect.h#L73) module in [`python/triton/runtime/cache.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/runtime/cache.py), which supports both local and remote storage options.  
这些自动调优和启发式功能与 Triton 的 JIT 编译和内核执行流程无缝集成，如 JIT 编译、缓存和内核执行所述。位于 `python/triton/runtime/jit.py` 的 `JITFunction` 类通过处理参数解析、特化和优化内核的最终启动，发挥着核心作用。由 `python/triton/runtime/driver.py` 中的 `driver` 管理的运行时环境，确保所选配置应用于适当的后端执行。编译工件的缓存，包括调优结果，由 `python/triton/runtime/cache.py` 中的 `cache` 模块处理，该模块支持本地和远程存储选项。

### Experimental Gluon Frontend and Hardware Abstraction  
实验性 Gluon 前端和硬件抽象

link

zoom\_in

The experimental Gluon frontend extends Triton's capabilities by offering lower-level, hardware-specific control for advanced GPU architectures, including NVIDIA Hopper and Blackwell, as well as AMD GPUs. This is achieved through specialized Intermediate Representation (IR) dialects, custom memory layouts, and fine-grained control over hardware operations.  
实验性的 Gluon 前端通过提供针对高级 GPU 架构（包括 NVIDIA Hopper 和 Blackwell，以及 AMD GPU）的更低层次、硬件特定的控制来扩展 Triton 的功能。这是通过专门的中间表示（IR）方言、自定义内存布局以及对硬件操作的细粒度控制来实现的。

Gluon integrates a dedicated JIT compilation path that converts Python Abstract Syntax Trees (ASTs) of Triton kernels into Triton IR with [`GLUON`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/backends/compiler.py#L20) backend attributes, as detailed in [`python/triton/experimental/gluon/_runtime.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/_runtime.py). This ensures that Gluon-specific metadata and optimizations are incorporated early in the compilation process.  
Gluon 集成了一个专用的 JIT 编译路径，将 Triton 内核的 Python 抽象语法树（ASTs）转换为带有 `GLUON` 后端属性的 Triton IR，具体细节见 `python/triton/experimental/gluon/_runtime.py` 。这确保了 Gluon 特定的元数据和优化在编译过程中尽早被整合。

The Gluon language features, defined in [`python/triton/experimental/gluon/language`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language), provide specialized value and type definitions, primitive data types, and core API functions. These functionalities facilitate distributed tensor operations, shared memory management, and direct control over hardware resources. Memory management is enhanced with utilities for allocating shared memory and creating shared memory descriptors. Additionally, various layout strategies, such as [`AutoLayout`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/_layouts.py#L32), [`BlockedLayout`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/_layouts.py#L60), and [`SwizzledSharedLayout`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/_layouts.py#L456), are available to optimize memory access patterns. The Gluon semantic model, specifically [`GluonSemantic`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/_semantic.py#L98) in [`python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/_semantic.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/_semantic.py), manages distributed types, layouts, and warp specialization, enabling the construction of Gluon IR operations.  
Gluon 语言特性，定义在 `python/triton/experimental/gluon/language` 中，提供了专门的值和类型定义、原始数据类型和核心 API 函数。这些功能促进了分布式张量操作、共享内存管理和对硬件资源的直接控制。内存管理通过分配共享内存和创建共享内存描述符的工具得到增强。此外，还有多种布局策略，如 `AutoLayout` 、 `BlockedLayout` 和 `SwizzledSharedLayout` ，可用于优化内存访问模式。Gluon 语义模型，特别是 `GluonSemantic` 在 `python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/_semantic.py` 中的实现，管理分布式类型、布局和 warp 专业化，能够构建 Gluon IR 操作。

For NVIDIA GPUs, the Gluon framework provides architecture-specific functionalities for Hopper and Blackwell within [`python/triton/experimental/gluon/nvidia`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/nvidia). This includes specialized [`TensorDescriptor`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/tools/tensor_descriptor.py#L7) classes, such as [`TensorDescriptorIm2Col`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/nvidia/hopper.py#L107), which are used to represent tensor metadata and optimize memory access for tiled and [`im2col`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/ir.cc#L197) operations. The subdirectory [`python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/nvidia`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/nvidia) further defines operations like [`mma_v2`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/nvidia/ampere/__init__.py#L13) for matrix multiply-accumulate on Ampere, and advanced features such as Tensor Memory (TMEM) operations ([`tcgen05_copy`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/nvidia/blackwell/__init__.py#L445), [`tcgen05_mma`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/nvidia/blackwell/__init__.py#L459)) and Cluster Launch Control (CLC) for Blackwell. TMA (Tensor Memory Accelerator) operations, such as [`async_copy_global_to_shared`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/nvidia/hopper/tma.py#L189), and mbarrier synchronization primitives are also available for efficient asynchronous data transfers and inter-warp/CTA coordination on Hopper and Blackwell architectures.  
对于 NVIDIA GPU，Gluon 框架在 `python/triton/experimental/gluon/nvidia` 中为 Hopper 和 Blackwell 提供了特定于架构的功能。这包括专门用于表示张量元数据和优化 tiling 及 `im2col` 操作的 `TensorDescriptor` 类，例如 `TensorDescriptorIm2Col` 。子目录 `python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/nvidia` 进一步定义了 Ampere 上的矩阵乘累加操作 `mma_v2` ，以及 Blackwell 的高级功能，如 Tensor Memory (TMEM)操作（ `tcgen05_copy` ， `tcgen05_mma` ）和 Cluster Launch Control (CLC)。TMA（Tensor Memory Accelerator）操作，如 `async_copy_global_to_shared` ，以及 mbarrier 同步原语也提供，用于在 Hopper 和 Blackwell 架构上高效地进行异步数据传输和跨 warp/CTA 协调。

Similarly, for AMD GPUs, the Gluon framework includes specific support for architectures like [`gfx1250`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/gluon_ir.cc#L172), as found in [`python/triton/experimental/gluon/amd`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/amd). This backend provides [`TensorDescriptor`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/tools/tensor_descriptor.py#L7) structures with layout and blocking information to optimize memory access. The subdirectory [`python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/amd`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/amd) offers architecture-specific layouts like [`AMDMFMALayout`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/amd/_layouts.py#L16) and [`AMDWMMALayout`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/amd/_layouts.py#L108), alongside buffer operations, matrix core operations ([`mfma`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/unittest/Dialect/TritonGPU/LinearLayoutConversionsTest.cpp#L62), [`wmma`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/unittest/Dialect/TritonGPU/LinearLayoutConversionsTest.cpp#L82)), asynchronous memory copies, and mbarrier synchronization tailored for AMD hardware.  
类似地，对于 AMD GPU，Gluon 框架为 `gfx1250` 等架构提供了特定支持，如 `python/triton/experimental/gluon/amd` 中所示。这个后端为 `TensorDescriptor` 结构提供布局和分块信息以优化内存访问。子目录 `python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/amd` 提供了针对 AMD 硬件的特定布局，如 `AMDMFMALayout` 和 `AMDWMMALayout` ，以及缓冲区操作、矩阵核心操作（ `mfma` ， `wmma` ）、异步内存复制和为 AMD 硬件定制的 mbarrier 同步。

The integration of these hardware-specific features and specialized IR dialects, as exemplified in the [`python/examples/gluon`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon) directory, allows developers to achieve fine-grained control over GPU operations. This enables the creation of highly optimized kernels for deep learning tasks, leveraging techniques such as multi-CTA cooperation, shared memory tiling, and advanced synchronization mechanisms to maximize performance on targeted GPU architectures.  
这些特定于硬件的功能和专用中间表示方言的集成，以 `python/examples/gluon` 目录中的示例为代表，使开发者能够对 GPU 操作实现细粒度控制。这能够为深度学习任务创建高度优化的内核，利用多 CTA 协作、共享内存 tiling 和高级同步机制等技术，以在目标 GPU 架构上最大化性能。

## Deep Learning Kernels and Examples  
深度学习内核和示例

link

zoom\_in

Triton provides highly optimized deep learning kernels designed for execution on GPUs, encompassing foundational operations like matrix multiplication, attention mechanisms, convolutions, and layer normalization. These kernels demonstrate how to leverage Triton's capabilities for high-performance GPU-accelerated operations, including advanced topics such as Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models and distributed communication.  
Triton 提供了为 GPU 执行而高度优化的深度学习内核，涵盖了矩阵乘法、注意力机制、卷积和层归一化等基础操作。这些内核展示了如何利用 Triton 的功能实现高性能 GPU 加速操作，包括 Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) 模型和分布式通信等高级主题。

The core kernels are found in the [`triton_kernels`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/Makefile#L37) module. This module implements functionalities such as tensor compaction for efficient memory use, distributed communication utilities for converting data between data-parallel and expert-parallel formats, and advanced matrix multiplication (GEMM) with support for fused operations and flexible precision. It also includes general reduction operations and top-k selection for sparse matrices. For instance, the [`matmul`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/09-persistent-matmul.py#L162) function in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul.py) is Triton-optimized for various inputs, handling fused operations and ragged tensors, and dispatches to specific Triton kernels depending on the configuration. Similarly, SwiGLU activation is implemented in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/swiglu.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/swiglu.py) using a Triton kernel to integrate with [`torch.autograd`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/05-layer-norm.py#L233).  
核心内核位于 `triton_kernels` 模块中。该模块实现了多种功能，包括用于高效内存使用的张量压缩、用于在数据并行和专家并行格式之间转换数据的分布式通信工具，以及支持融合操作和灵活精度的先进矩阵乘法（GEMM）。它还包括通用归约操作和稀疏矩阵的 top-k 选择。例如， `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul.py` 中的 `matmul` 函数针对各种输入进行了 Triton 优化，处理融合操作和锯齿形张量，并根据配置调度到特定的 Triton 内核。类似地，SwiGLU 激活函数在 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/swiglu.py` 中通过 Triton 内核实现，以与 `torch.autograd` 集成。

For highly specialized applications, particularly targeting NVIDIA Blackwell GPUs, Triton offers an experimental Gluon API. This API provides fine-grained control over GPU hardware, enabling advanced techniques such as multi-CTA cooperation, shared memory tiling, and asynchronous data transfers via Tensor Memory Accelerator (TMA). Examples in [`python/examples/gluon`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon) showcase these capabilities, including optimized implementations of scaled dot-product attention, 2D convolution with TMA [`im2col`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/ir.cc#L197), and multi-CTA matrix multiplication kernels. These examples utilize features like hardware barriers ([`mbarrier`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/gluon_ir.cc#L658)) and specialized aggregates for managing synchronization and data flow. For example, the [`attention_kernel`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon/01-attention-forward.py#L828) in [`python/examples/gluon/01-attention-forward.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon/01-attention-forward.py) uses warp specialization and TMA for efficient data movement and computation.  
对于高度专业化的应用，特别是针对 NVIDIA Blackwell GPU，Triton 提供了一种实验性的 Gluon API。该 API 提供了对 GPU 硬件的细粒度控制，能够实现高级技术，如多 CTA 协作、共享内存 tiling 以及通过 Tensor Memory Accelerator（TMA）进行异步数据传输。 `python/examples/gluon` 中的示例展示了这些功能，包括优化实现的缩放点积注意力机制、使用 TMA 的 2D 卷积 `im2col` 以及多 CTA 矩阵乘法内核。这些示例利用了硬件屏障（ `mbarrier` ）和专门聚合等特性来管理同步和数据流。例如， `python/examples/gluon/01-attention-forward.py` 中的 `attention_kernel` 使用 warp 特化和 TMA 进行高效的数据移动和计算。

To assess the performance and correctness of these kernels, a comprehensive benchmarking and testing framework is available. This framework is used to evaluate distributed MoE MLP models, analyze performance using roofline plots, and validate various quantization schemes. The [`bench_mlp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/bench/bench_mlp.py#L89) function in [`python/triton_kernels/bench/bench_mlp.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/bench/bench_mlp.py) orchestrates these benchmarks, utilizing [`triton.profiler`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/setup.py#L399) for detailed tracing and [`torch.cuda.CUDAGraph`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/testing.py#L105) for stable performance measurements. Test suites, such as those in [`python/triton_kernels/tests`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/tests), ensure the accuracy and efficiency of the [`matmul`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/09-persistent-matmul.py#L162), [`mxfp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/TritonGPU/combine.mlir#L3728), [`distributed`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Analysis/Utility.cpp#L28), [`reduce`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1215), [`topk`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/topk.py#L88), and [`swiglu`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/swiglu.py#L25) kernels against PyTorch reference implementations. The testing infrastructure also provides fixtures for isolating Triton knob settings and managing distributed GPU assignments during testing.  
为了评估这些内核的性能和正确性，提供了一个全面的基准测试和测试框架。该框架用于评估分布式 MoE MLP 模型，使用屋顶线图分析性能，并验证各种量化方案。在 `bench_mlp` 中的 `python/triton_kernels/bench/bench_mlp.py` 函数协调这些基准测试，利用 `triton.profiler` 进行详细跟踪，并使用 `torch.cuda.CUDAGraph` 进行稳定的性能测量。测试套件，如 `python/triton_kernels/tests` 中的那些，确保 `matmul` 、 `mxfp` 、 `distributed` 、 `reduce` 、 `topk` 和 `swiglu` 内核相对于 PyTorch 参考实现的准确性和效率。测试基础设施还提供了用于隔离 Triton 旋钮设置和管理测试期间分布式 GPU 分配的固定装置。

### Triton-Optimized Kernels for Deep Learning  
深度学习优化的 Triton 内核

link

zoom\_in

The [`triton_kernels`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/Makefile#L37) module, located in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels), provides a collection of highly optimized kernel implementations leveraging Triton for GPU acceleration. These kernels are designed for fundamental deep learning operations, incorporating features such as flexible precision, efficient memory management, and specialized handling for distributed training scenarios.  
位于 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels` 的 `triton_kernels` 模块，提供了一系列利用 Triton 进行 GPU 加速的高度优化的内核实现。这些内核设计用于基本的深度学习操作，包括灵活的精度、高效的内存管理和针对分布式训练场景的专门处理。

Key functionalities include:  
主要功能包括：

-   **Tensor Compaction**: Operations for compacting data based on a bitmask, reorganizing values and indices while preserving order. This is implemented through the [`compaction`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/compaction.py#L6) function in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/compaction.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/compaction.py), which utilizes a Triton kernel, and a PyTorch reference for comparison.  
    张量紧缩：基于位掩码压缩数据的操作，重新组织值和索引同时保持顺序。这通过 `compaction` 中的 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/compaction.py` 函数实现，该函数使用 Triton 内核，并提供一个 PyTorch 参考实现用于比较。
-   **Distributed Operations**: Tools for managing expert assignments in distributed Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models and for converting data between data-parallel and expert-parallel representations. This includes [`ExptAssignment`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py#L10) structures and conversion functions like [`convert_dp_to_ep`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py#L176) and [`convert_ep_to_dp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py#L256) in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py). These conversions rely on a [`SymmetricMemoryPool`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed_details/mesh.py#L34) for efficient shared buffer management across distributed ranks. More details on these distributed MoE kernels and memory management can be found in [Distributed MoE Kernels and Memory Management](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#deep-learning-kernels-and-examples-triton-optimized-kernels-for-deep-learning-distributed-moe-kernels-and-memory-management).  
    分布式操作：用于管理分布式专家混合（MoE）模型中的专家分配，以及用于在数据并行和专家并行表示之间转换数据的工具。这包括 `ExptAssignment` 结构和 `convert_dp_to_ep` 、 `convert_ep_to_dp` 等转换函数，这些函数位于 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py` 中。这些转换依赖于 `SymmetricMemoryPool` 以实现跨分布式节点的有效共享缓冲区管理。有关这些分布式 MoE 内核和内存管理的更多详细信息，请参阅分布式 MoE 内核和内存管理。
-   **Matrix Multiplication (Matmul)**: A highly optimized [`matmul`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/09-persistent-matmul.py#L162) implementation that supports fused operations, flexible numerical precision, and advanced memory management techniques, including handling ragged tensors. The [`matmul`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/09-persistent-matmul.py#L162) function in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul.py) dynamically selects and configures Triton kernels, managing Triton Memory Allocators (TMAs) and supporting distributed communication patterns. For further details on these optimizations, refer to [Advanced Matrix Multiplication (Matmul) Optimizations](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#deep-learning-kernels-and-examples-triton-optimized-kernels-for-deep-learning-advanced-matrix-multiplication-matmul-optimizations).  
    矩阵乘法（Matmul）：一种高度优化的 `matmul` 实现，支持融合操作、灵活的数值精度和高级内存管理技术，包括处理不规则张量。 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul.py` 中的 `matmul` 函数动态选择和配置 Triton 内核，管理 Triton 内存分配器（TMAs），并支持分布式通信模式。有关这些优化的更多详细信息，请参阅高级矩阵乘法（Matmul）优化。
-   **General Reduction**: A flexible sum reduction operation for 3D tensors, supporting masking, scaling, and flexible floating-point (flexpoint) numerical formats. This includes both forward and backward passes, integrated with PyTorch's autograd system, defined in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/reduce.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/reduce.py).  
    通用缩减：一种灵活的 3D 张量求和缩减操作，支持掩码、缩放和灵活的浮点数（flexpoint）数值格式。这包括前向和后向传播，与 PyTorch 的自动微分系统集成，定义在 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/reduce.py` 。
-   **SwiGLU Activation**: An optimized implementation of the SwiGLU activation function with a focus on numerical stability and performance, particularly for flexpoint data types. The core logic is in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/swiglu_details/_swiglu.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/swiglu_details/_swiglu.py), featuring specialized [`exp_ftz`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/swiglu_details/_swiglu.py#L39) approximations.  
    SwiGLU 激活函数：一种针对 SwiGLU 激活函数的优化实现，重点在于数值稳定性和性能，尤其适用于 flexpoint 数据类型。核心逻辑位于 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/swiglu_details/_swiglu.py` ，包含专门的 `exp_ftz` 近似方法。
-   **Top-K Selection**: Kernels for stable streaming top-k selection, including floating-point keying, index tie-breaking, optional softmax application, and gradient computation. The forward and backward passes are implemented in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/topk_details/_topk_forward.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/topk_details/_topk_forward.py) and [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/topk_details/_topk_backward.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/topk_details/_topk_backward.py) respectively.  
    Top-K 选择：用于稳定流式 Top-K 选择的内核，包括浮点数键值、索引平局决断、可选的 Softmax 应用和梯度计算。前向和后向传递分别由 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/topk_details/_topk_forward.py` 和 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/topk_details/_topk_backward.py` 实现。

The module also includes comprehensive support for [Flexible and Mixed Precision Numerics](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#deep-learning-kernels-and-examples-triton-optimized-kernels-for-deep-learning-flexible-and-mixed-precision-numerics), defining data structures for flexible tensor representation ([`InFlexData`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics.py#L27), [`OutFlexData`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics.py#L36) in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics.py)) and providing Triton kernels for flexpoint and MXFP operations (in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details)). These numeric implementations include type-specific constants, conversion functions between float and flexpoint/MXFP formats, and dynamic scale management, alongside optimized CUDA-specific reductions.  
该模块还包含对灵活和混合精度数值的全面支持，定义了用于灵活张量表示的数据结构（在 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics.py` 中的 `InFlexData` 和 `OutFlexData` ），并提供用于 flexpoint 和 MXFP 操作的 Triton 内核（在 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details` 中）。这些数值实现包括特定类型的常量、在 float 和 flexpoint/MXFP 格式之间进行转换的函数，以及动态比例管理，同时还包括针对 CUDA 的优化归约操作。

Underlying these kernels are specialized utility functions and data structures for managing tensor data types, memory layouts, and metadata for complex structures like bitmatrices and ragged tensors, as detailed in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/tensor_details`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/tensor_details). These components enable hardware-aware optimizations for NVIDIA and AMD GPUs, utilizing Triton JIT compilation for performance. The [`Closure`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/meta.py#L6) [`NamedTuple`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/_utils.py#L152) in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/meta.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/meta.py) facilitates the capture of functions and their environment, enabling flexible and expressive kernel programming.  
在这些内核之下是用于管理张量数据类型、内存布局以及位矩阵和稀疏张量等复杂结构的元数据和专用工具函数，具体细节请参考 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/tensor_details` 。这些组件能够为 NVIDIA 和 AMD GPU 实现硬件感知优化，并利用 Triton JIT 编译来提升性能。在 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/meta.py` 中的 `Closure` `NamedTuple` 能够捕获函数及其环境，从而实现灵活且表达力强的内核编程。

#### Flexible and Mixed Precision Numerics  
灵活和混合精度数值

link

zoom\_in

Triton's numerical kernels are designed to leverage flexible floating-point (flexpoint) and mixed-precision floating-point (MXFP) formats to optimize deep learning models by improving memory efficiency and computational speed. These kernels handle various data types, including [`FP4`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/tensor_details/dtype.py#L27), [`FP8_E4M3FN`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/tensor_details/dtype.py#L28), [`FP8_E5M2`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/tensor_details/dtype.py#L30), and [`float16`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L821).  
Triton 的数值内核旨在利用灵活浮点（flexpoint）和混合精度浮点（MXFP）格式，通过提高内存效率和计算速度来优化深度学习模型。这些内核处理多种数据类型，包括 `FP4` 、 `FP8_E4M3FN` 、 `FP8_E5M2` 和 `float16` 。

The system includes mechanisms for converting between standard floating-point types and these specialized formats. This involves dynamic scale management, where scaling factors are computed and applied to prevent overflow and maintain numerical precision during conversion. Kernels such as those found in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details/flexpoint.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details/flexpoint.py) provide functionalities to retrieve type-specific maximum finite values and their reciprocals, which are essential for clamping and scaling operations.  
该系统包含在标准浮点类型和这些专用格式之间进行转换的机制。这涉及动态比例管理，其中计算并应用缩放因子以防止溢出并在转换过程中保持数值精度。像 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details/flexpoint.py` 中找到的那些内核提供功能来检索特定类型的最大有限值及其倒数，这对于夹断和缩放操作至关重要。

For mixed-precision operations, Triton offers both highly optimized JIT-compiled kernels and pure PyTorch implementations for flexibility. Quantization (downcasting) converts higher-precision tensors into MXFP formats by calculating and applying per-group scales. Conversely, dequantization (upcasting) reconstructs higher-precision tensors from MXFP formats using stored scaling factors. The choice of rounding mode for dequantization scales, such as [`ROUND_UP`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details/mxfp.py#L20) or [`ROUND_DOWN`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details/mxfp.py#L23), impacts numerical precision and potential value clipping. The core logic for these conversions is found in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details/mxfp.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details/mxfp.py) and its associated detailed kernels in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details/mxfp_details`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details/mxfp_details).  
对于混合精度操作，Triton 提供了高度优化的 JIT 编译内核和纯 PyTorch 实现，以提供灵活性。量化（向下转型）通过计算和应用每组的缩放因子，将高精度张量转换为 MXFP 格式。相反，去量化（向上转型）使用存储的缩放因子，从 MXFP 格式重建高精度张量。去量化缩放的舍入模式选择，如 `ROUND_UP` 或 `ROUND_DOWN` ，会影响数值精度和潜在值裁剪。这些转换的核心逻辑位于 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details/mxfp.py` 中，以及 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/numerics_details/mxfp_details` 中相关的详细内核。

The implementation adapts to different GPU architectures, utilizing inline PTX assembly for efficient FP4 conversion on newer NVIDIA CUDA devices while providing robust software fallbacks for broader compatibility. This dual-path approach ensures that performance-critical operations benefit from hardware acceleration when available, without sacrificing compatibility on older hardware. Operations like matrix multiplication and attention mechanisms leverage these flexible precision numerics to achieve high performance. See [Advanced Matrix Multiplication (Matmul) Optimizations](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#deep-learning-kernels-and-examples-triton-optimized-kernels-for-deep-learning-advanced-matrix-multiplication-matmul-optimizations) for more details.  
该实现适应不同的 GPU 架构，利用内联 PTX 汇编在新一代 NVIDIA CUDA 设备上进行高效的 FP4 转换，同时提供稳健的软件回退方案以实现更广泛的兼容性。这种双路径方法确保在硬件加速可用时，性能关键的操作能够受益于硬件加速，而不会牺牲旧硬件的兼容性。矩阵乘法和注意力机制等操作利用这些灵活的精度数值技术来达到高性能。更多详情请参阅高级矩阵乘法（Matmul）优化。

#### Distributed MoE Kernels and Memory Management  
分布式 MoE 内核与内存管理

link

zoom\_in

Distributed Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models necessitate specialized kernels and memory management to efficiently handle data across multiple processing units. Triton addresses this through mechanisms for expert assignment and data conversion between data-parallel (DP) and expert-parallel (EP) formats, leveraging symmetric memory pooling for shared buffers.  
分布式专家混合（MoE）模型需要专门的内核和内存管理来高效处理跨多个处理单元的数据。Triton 通过专家分配和数据转换机制（在数据并行，DP 格式和专家并行，EP 格式之间）来解决这个问题，利用对称内存池化来管理共享缓冲区。

Expert assignment, managed by the [`ExptAssignment`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py#L10) dataclass in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py), defines which experts are processed by which GPU or rank. This includes a bitmask for ownership, a boolean mask, and a mapping from global to local expert IDs. Functions like [`make_expt_dict_uniform`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py#L25) and [`make_expt_dict_random`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py#L38) facilitate distributing experts, either uniformly or randomly, ensuring each expert is owned by a single shard.  
专家分配由 `ExptAssignment` 数据类在 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py` 中管理，定义了哪些专家由哪个 GPU 或 rank 处理。这包括所有权位掩码、布尔掩码以及从全局到本地专家 ID 的映射。 `make_expt_dict_uniform` 和 `make_expt_dict_random` 等函数促进专家的分配，可以是均匀分配或随机分配，确保每个专家只属于单个分片。

Data conversion between DP and EP representations is critical for MoE. Triton provides kernels, defined in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py), to move data from a DP format, where all data is available on each processing unit, to an EP format, where tokens are routed to specific experts on different processing units. Conversely, EP data is converted back to DP format after expert processing. These kernels determine which tokens belong to which peer GPU based on expert ownership and manage data transfer to the correct destinations.  
在 DP 和 EP 表示形式之间的数据转换对 MoE 至关重要。Triton 提供了在 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py` 中定义的内核，用于将数据从 DP 格式（所有数据在每个处理单元上可用）转换到 EP 格式（标记被路由到不同处理单元上的特定专家）。相反，在专家处理完成后，EP 数据会转换回 DP 格式。这些内核根据专家所有权确定哪些标记属于哪个同伴 GPU，并管理数据传输到正确的目的地。

Underlying these operations is the concept of symmetric memory pooling, which is managed by the [`SymmetricMemoryPool`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed_details/mesh.py#L34) class, primarily defined in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed_details/mesh.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed_details/mesh.py). This pool allows for the allocation and management of shared memory regions across distributed processes. It uses a [`Mesh`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed_details/mesh.py#L13) object to encapsulate distributed process group information, including world size and local rank. [`SymmetricMemoryPool`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed_details/mesh.py#L34) can reserve named memory regions and allocate [`torch.Tensor`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/specialize.cc#L474) objects from these regions, ensuring correct alignment and size. For distributed environments, it coordinates shared access across processes using [`symm_mem.empty`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed_details/mesh.py#L127) and [`symm_mem.rendezvous`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed_details/mesh.py#L128), and retrieves local views of buffers. A specialized method, [`initialize_matmul`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed_details/mesh.py#L138), reserves memory for distributed matrix multiplication, calculating buffer sizes for "topk," "ep\_to\_dp," and "dp\_to\_ep" operations, which are then used to set up the symmetric memory for efficient data exchange. This symmetric memory management is crucial for minimizing communication overhead and enabling efficient distributed tensor operations.  
这些操作的基础是对称内存池的概念，由 `SymmetricMemoryPool` 类管理，主要定义在 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed_details/mesh.py` 中。这个池允许跨分布式进程分配和管理共享内存区域。它使用 `Mesh` 对象封装分布式进程组信息，包括世界大小和本地秩。 `SymmetricMemoryPool` 可以预留命名内存区域，并从这些区域分配 `torch.Tensor` 对象，确保正确的对齐和大小。对于分布式环境，它使用 `symm_mem.empty` 和 `symm_mem.rendezvous` 协调进程间的共享访问，并获取缓冲区的本地视图。一个特殊的方法 `initialize_matmul` 为分布式矩阵乘法预留内存，计算 "topk"、"ep\_to\_dp" 和 "dp\_to\_ep" 操作的缓冲区大小，然后用于设置对称内存以实现高效数据交换。这种对称内存管理对于最小化通信开销和实现高效的分布式张量操作至关重要。

#### Advanced Matrix Multiplication (Matmul) Optimizations  
高级矩阵乘法（Matmul）优化

link

zoom\_in

Triton's matrix multiplication (Matmul) kernels incorporate several optimizations to achieve high performance across different GPU architectures. These optimizations include dynamic configuration, flexible precision handling, support for ragged tensors, and fused operations.  
Triton 的矩阵乘法（Matmul）内核包含多种优化，以在不同 GPU 架构上实现高性能。这些优化包括动态配置、灵活的精度处理、对不规则张量的支持以及融合操作。

A central component for defining these operations is the [`_matmul`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_matmul.py#L30) kernel, found in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_matmul.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_matmul.py), which is a configurable General Matrix Multiplication (GEMM) operation. This kernel leverages Triton's Just-In-Time (JIT) compilation to generate efficient code. A parallel version, [`_p_matmul`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_p_matmul.py#L58) in [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_p_matmul.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_p_matmul.py), extends this functionality with further customization and architectural-specific tuning.
