定义这些操作的核心组件是 `_matmul` 内核，位于 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_matmul.py` 中，它是一种可配置的通用矩阵乘法（GEMM）操作。该内核利用 Triton 的即时编译（JIT）技术生成高效代码。一个并行版本， `_p_matmul` 位于 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_p_matmul.py` 中，通过进一步的自定义和针对特定架构的微调扩展了此功能。

**Dynamic Configuration for GPU Architectures  
GPU 架构的动态配置**

The system dynamically configures kernel launch parameters and block dimensions based on the target GPU architecture (NVIDIA or AMD) and input tensor properties. This is managed by the functions within [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags.py). This module determines optimal [`OptFlags`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags.py#L16) such as [`block_m`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon/02-convolution.py#L76), [`block_n`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon/02-convolution.py#L77), [`block_k`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon/02-convolution.py#L78) (matrix block dimensions), [`num_warps`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/knobs.py#L437), [`num_stages`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/knobs.py#L439), and [`split_k`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags.py#L25) (for K-dimension tiling). The selection process is influenced by factors like tensor dimensions, data types, and hardware capabilities, including specific AMD CDNA/RDNA versions or NVIDIA CUDA compute capabilities. Helper modules within [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details), such as [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details/opt_flags_amd.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details/opt_flags_amd.py) and [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details/opt_flags_nvidia.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details/opt_flags_nvidia.py), provide architecture-specific logic for these calculations. For instance, [`compute_block_nk`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details/opt_flags_amd.py#L6) for AMD GPUs calculates optimal [`block_n`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon/02-convolution.py#L77) and [`block_k`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon/02-convolution.py#L78), while [`compute_grid_size`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details/opt_flags_nvidia.py#L16), [`compute_block_n`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details/opt_flags_nvidia.py#L25), [`compute_block_k`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details/opt_flags_nvidia.py#L44), [`compute_split_k`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details/opt_flags_nvidia.py#L67), [`compute_num_warps`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details/opt_flags_nvidia.py#L79), and [`compute_num_stages`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details/opt_flags_nvidia.py#L89) determine parameters tailored for NVIDIA GPUs, considering features like Hopper and Blackwell micro-scaled layouts.  
系统根据目标 GPU 架构（NVIDIA 或 AMD）和输入张量属性动态配置内核启动参数和块维度。这由 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags.py` 中的函数管理。该模块确定最优的 `OptFlags` ，例如 `block_m` 、 `block_n` 、 `block_k` （矩阵块维度）、 `num_warps` 、 `num_stages` 和 `split_k` （用于 K 维度瓦片）。选择过程受张量维度、数据类型和硬件能力等因素影响，包括特定的 AMD CDNA/RDNA 版本或 NVIDIA CUDA 计算能力。 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details` 中的辅助模块，如 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details/opt_flags_amd.py` 和 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags_details/opt_flags_nvidia.py` ，为这些计算提供架构特定的逻辑。例如，AMD GPU 的 `compute_block_nk` 计算 `block_n` 和 `block_k` 的最优值，而 `compute_grid_size` 、 `compute_block_n` 、 `compute_block_k` 、 `compute_split_k` 、 `compute_num_warps` 和 `compute_num_stages` 确定针对 NVIDIA GPU 的参数，考虑 Hopper 和 Blackwell 微架构布局等特性。

**Flexible Precision Handling  
灵活的精度处理**

Triton's Matmul kernels support various floating-point formats, including mixed-precision (MXFP8/MXFP4) and FlexPoint. The kernels manage scaling factors for different precision types and micro-scaling, which is critical for efficiency in deep learning models. This involves explicit checks for micro-scaled inputs and outputs ([`is_x_microscaled`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_matmul.py#L115), [`is_w_microscaled`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_matmul.py#L116), [`is_out_microscaled`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_matmul.py#L166)) and the application of specific swizzling logic for architectures like NVIDIA Blackwell and Hopper to correctly interpret scaled data layouts. The [`tl.dot_scaled`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/10-block-scaled-matmul.py#L63) primitive is used for scaled dot products when micro-scaling is enabled. Furthermore, FlexPoint scaling for output precision is supported, with mechanisms for dynamically computing or applying scales as needed.  
Triton 的 Matmul 内核支持多种浮点数格式，包括混合精度（MXFP8/MXFP4）和 FlexPoint。这些内核管理不同精度类型的缩放因子和微缩放，这对深度学习模型的效率至关重要。这包括对微缩放输入和输出（ `is_x_microscaled` ， `is_w_microscaled` ， `is_out_microscaled` ）进行显式检查，以及对 NVIDIA Blackwell 和 Hopper 等架构应用特定的 swizzling 逻辑，以正确解释缩放数据布局。当启用微缩放时， `tl.dot_scaled` 原语用于缩放点积。此外，还支持输出精度的 FlexPoint 缩放，并具有根据需要动态计算或应用缩放机制。

**Support for Ragged Tensors  
对齐张量的支持**

The Matmul kernels can handle ragged (non-uniform) tensor dimensions, which are common in models such as Mixture-of-Experts (MoE). This is managed by parameters like [`RAGGED_DIMENSION`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_common.py#L86) and associated slice size/offset arrays ([`XSliceSizes`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_common.py#L181), [`XSliceOffs`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_common.py#L80), [`WSliceSizes`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_matmul.py#L50), [`WSliceOffs`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_common.py#L84)). The [`compute_offsets`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_common.py#L75) function within [`python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_common.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_common.py) plays a role in calculating memory offsets for input and weight tensors, enabling correct memory access despite irregular dimensions.  
Matmul 内核可以处理锯齿形（非均匀）张量维度，这在 Mixture-of-Experts（MoE）等模型中很常见。这是通过 `RAGGED_DIMENSION` 等参数以及相关的切片大小/偏移数组（ `XSliceSizes` 、 `XSliceOffs` 、 `WSliceSizes` 、 `WSliceOffs` ）来管理的。 `python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/_common.py` 中的 `compute_offsets` 函数在计算输入和权重张量的内存偏移方面发挥作用，使得即使维度不规则也能正确进行内存访问。

**Fused Operations and Persistent Kernels  
融合操作和持久内核**

The kernels integrate fused operations, allowing for the application of bias, activation functions, and post-multiplication epilogues directly within the GEMM computation. This minimizes memory transfers and improves overall efficiency. User-defined [`ACTIVATION_FN`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul.py#L73) and [`EPILOGUE_FN`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul.py#L72) parameters, passed as [`tl.constexpr`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/README.md?plain=1#L55) arguments, enable flexible customization of these post-processing steps.  
内核集成了融合操作，允许在 GEMM 计算中直接应用偏差、激活函数和后乘法尾声。这最小化了内存传输并提高了整体效率。用户定义的 `ACTIVATION_FN` 和 `EPILOGUE_FN` 参数，作为 `tl.constexpr` 参数传递，能够灵活地定制这些后处理步骤。

For NVIDIA GPUs, the concept of "persistent kernels" is used, where the kernel remains resident on the GPU and continuously processes work. This is determined by the [`is_persistent`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags.py#L26) flag in the [`OptFlags`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags.py#L16) and depends on factors like [`can_use_persistent_tma`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul_details/opt_flags.py#L60), memory layouts, and estimated GPU occupancy. Persistent kernels are particularly beneficial for workloads with consistent, high throughput.  
对于 NVIDIA GPU，使用“持久内核”的概念，其中内核驻留在 GPU 上并持续处理工作。这由 `is_persistent` 和 `OptFlags` 中的 `is_persistent` 标志决定，并取决于因素如 `can_use_persistent_tma` 、内存布局和估计的 GPU 占用率。持久内核特别适用于具有稳定、高吞吐量的工作负载。

**Advanced Features  高级功能**

The Matmul kernels also incorporate features like [`SPLIT_K`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/python/examples/gluon/mxfp_fa_gfx1250.py#L461) for parallelization along the K-dimension, [`X_TMA_MODE`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul.py#L550) and [`Y_TMA_MODE`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul.py#L551) for Tensor Memory Accelerator (TMA) support on NVIDIA hardware, and fused communication via [`pYPtrs`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/matmul.py#L494) for distributed training scenarios. These capabilities contribute to high-performance tensor computations, particularly in machine learning workloads.  
Matmul 内核还集成了诸如 `SPLIT_K` 用于沿 K 维度并行化、 `X_TMA_MODE` 和 `Y_TMA_MODE` 用于 NVIDIA 硬件上的 Tensor Memory Accelerator (TMA)支持，以及通过 `pYPtrs` 进行融合通信以支持分布式训练场景等功能。这些特性有助于高性能张量计算，特别是在机器学习工作负载中。

### Experimental Gluon Kernels for Blackwell  
Blackwell 的 Gluon 内核实验

link

python

content\_copyCopy  复制

@gluon.jit def matmul\_load\_partition(p): \# ... (boilerplate for K and concurrent\_loads) scheduler = p.get\_clc\_consumer() i = 0 while scheduler.has\_work: off\_m, off\_n = scheduler.get\_offsets() for k in range(0, K, BLOCK\_K): \# ... (boilerplate for pred and mbarrier.wait) bar = p.load\_ready\_bars.index(state.index) \# Expects a specific byte count for the TMA copies to follow mbarrier.expect(bar, p.a\_desc.nbytes\_per\_cta + p.b\_desc.nbytes\_per\_cta) \# Asynchronously copy global memory to shared memory for matrix A tma.async\_copy\_global\_to\_shared(p.a\_desc, \[off\_m, k\], bar, p.a\_bufs.index(state.index), multicast=True) \# Asynchronously copy global memory to shared memory for matrix B tma.async\_copy\_global\_to\_shared(p.b\_desc, \[k, off\_n\], bar, p.b\_bufs.index(state.index), multicast=True) state = state.next() scheduler = scheduler.step(i) i += 1  
@gluon.jit def matmul\_load\_partition(p): # ... (boilerplate for K and concurrent\_loads) scheduler = p.get\_clc\_consumer() i = 0 while scheduler.has\_work: off\_m, off\_n = scheduler.get\_offsets() for k in range(0, K, BLOCK\_K): # ... (预定义和 mbarrier.wait 的模板) bar = p.load\_ready\_bars.index(state.index) # 期待接下来的 TMA 复制具有特定的字节数 mbarrier.expect(bar, p.a\_desc.nbytes\_per\_cta + p.b\_desc.nbytes\_per\_cta) # 异步将全局内存复制到共享内存，用于矩阵 A tma.async\_copy\_global\_to\_shared(p.a\_desc, \[off\_m, k\], bar, p.a\_bufs.index(state.index), multicast=True) # 异步将全局内存复制到共享内存，用于矩阵 B tma.async\_copy\_global\_to\_shared(p.b\_desc, \[k, off\_n\], bar, p.b\_bufs.index(state.index), multicast=True) state = state.next() scheduler = scheduler.step(i) i += 1

The experimental Gluon frontend provides lower-level, hardware-specific control for advanced GPU architectures, particularly NVIDIA Blackwell. This control enables fine-grained optimization of core deep learning operations such as attention mechanisms, convolutions, and matrix multiplication. The Gluon API facilitates advanced techniques like multi-CTA (Cooperative Thread Array) cooperation, shared memory tiling, and the use of Tensor Memory Accelerator (TMA) for asynchronous data transfers, along with hardware barriers for precise synchronization.  
实验性的 Gluon 前端为高级 GPU 架构（尤其是 NVIDIA Blackwell）提供了更低层级的、特定硬件的控制。这种控制能够对注意力机制、卷积和矩阵乘法等核心深度学习操作进行细粒度优化。Gluon API 支持多 CTA（协作线程数组）协作、共享内存瓦片等高级技术，以及使用张量内存加速器（TMA）进行异步数据传输，并配合硬件屏障实现精确同步。

For example, the implementation of scaled dot-product attention in [`python/examples/gluon/01-attention-forward.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon/01-attention-forward.py) demonstrates how Gluon is used to create a highly optimized forward pass. This kernel leverages warp specialization to orchestrate sub-kernels for loading, matrix multiplication, and softmax computation, employing Blackwell-specific features like [`mbarrier`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/gluon_ir.cc#L658) for synchronization and [`tma.async_copy_global_to_shared`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/gluon/04-tma.py#L96) for efficient data movement. The [`Channel`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon/01-attention-forward.py#L63) factory in this implementation is a key component for managing multi-buffered producer-consumer communication using shared memory and [`mbarrier`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/gluon_ir.cc#L658)s, effectively pipelining data processing.  
例如， `python/examples/gluon/01-attention-forward.py` 中的缩放点积注意力实现展示了如何使用 Gluon 创建高度优化的前向传递。该内核利用 warp 专业化来协调加载、矩阵乘法和 softmax 计算的子内核，并采用 Blackwell 特有的功能，如 `mbarrier` 用于同步和 `tma.async_copy_global_to_shared` 用于高效数据移动。在此实现中， `Channel` 工厂是管理使用共享内存和 `mbarrier` 的多缓冲区生产者-消费者通信的关键组件，有效实现数据处理流水线。

Similarly, the 2D convolution kernel found in [`python/examples/gluon/02-convolution.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon/02-convolution.py) utilizes an implicit GEMM approach with TMA [`im2col`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/ir.cc#L197). This allows for efficient transformation of input data into a matrix format directly in shared memory, which is then processed by specialized matrix multiplication units. The convolution kernel also employs a pipelined execution model with distinct warp groups for loading, computing, and writing results, all synchronized by hardware barriers. This approach maximizes hardware utilization by overlapping memory operations with computation.  
类似地， `python/examples/gluon/02-convolution.py` 中的二维卷积核采用隐式 GEMM 方法，结合 TMA `im2col` 技术。这允许将输入数据高效地转换为矩阵格式，直接在共享内存中进行处理，然后由专用矩阵乘法单元进行处理。卷积核还采用流水线执行模型，使用不同的 warp 组分别进行加载、计算和写入结果，所有操作均通过硬件屏障同步。这种方法通过重叠内存操作与计算来最大化硬件利用率。

The matrix multiplication kernel in [`python/examples/gluon/03-matmul-multicta.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/examples/gluon/03-matmul-multicta.py) further illustrates the capabilities of Gluon for Blackwell GPUs. It supports multi-CTA cooperation, where multiple CTAs work collaboratively on different parts of the same matrix, managed through parameters like [`cga_layout`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/_layouts.py#L154). This implementation integrates advanced features such as [`tcgen05_mma`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/experimental/gluon/language/nvidia/blackwell/__init__.py#L459) for Blackwell Tensor Core operations, [`tma.async_copy_global_to_shared`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/gluon/04-tma.py#L96) for efficient data loading, and Cooperative Load and Cache (CLC) mechanisms for dynamic work scheduling across CTAs. The extensive use of [`aggregate`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/CMakeLists.txt#L192) classes and [`gl.constexpr`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/gluon/04-tma.py#L56) within these kernels allows for aggressive compile-time optimization and specialization, tailoring the code directly to the underlying hardware capabilities.  
`python/examples/gluon/03-matmul-multicta.py` 中的矩阵乘法内核进一步展示了 Gluon 在 Blackwell GPU 上的功能。它支持多 CTA 协作，多个 CTA 协同处理同一矩阵的不同部分，通过参数如 `cga_layout` 进行管理。该实现集成了高级特性，如 `tcgen05_mma` 用于 Blackwell Tensor Core 操作， `tma.async_copy_global_to_shared` 用于高效数据加载，以及用于跨 CTA 动态工作调度的协作加载和缓存（CLC）机制。这些内核中广泛使用 `aggregate` 类和 `gl.constexpr` ，允许在编译时进行激进优化和特化，直接将代码定制为底层硬件的能力。

### Performance Benchmarking and Testing Framework  
性能基准测试和测试框架

link

zoom\_in

The Triton framework includes a comprehensive system for benchmarking and testing its kernels, essential for verifying correctness and optimizing performance across various hardware configurations. This system supports roofline analysis for distributed Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) Multilayer Perceptron (MLP) models, provides extensive test suites, and offers mechanisms for configuring and isolating Triton's internal settings during evaluation.  
Triton 框架包含一个全面的系统，用于对其内核进行基准测试和测试，这对于在各种硬件配置中验证正确性和优化性能至关重要。该系统支持分布式专家混合（MoE）多层感知器（MLP）模型的屋顶线分析，提供广泛的测试套件，并提供了在评估期间配置和隔离 Triton 内部设置的机制。

The benchmarking component, primarily located in [`python/triton_kernels/bench`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/bench), focuses on evaluating distributed MoE MLP models. This involves analyzing performance, especially with different quantization schemes, and visualizing the results through roofline plots. Benchmarking is designed to run in a distributed environment, leveraging optimized Triton kernels. Key functions within this component include [`bench_mlp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/bench/bench_mlp.py#L89) which orchestrates single benchmark runs, managing memory pools, input tensors, and precision configurations. It also integrates with [`proton`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/knobs.py#L570) for detailed profiling and uses [`torch.cuda.CUDAGraph`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/testing.py#L105) to capture and replay computations for stable performance measurements. The [`roofline_mlp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/bench/bench_mlp.py#L177) function then consolidates these benchmarks to generate roofline plots, aiding in the analysis of computational intensity and memory bandwidth usage. For more details on the Proton framework, see [Proton Profiling Framework Overview](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#performance-profiling-and-debugging-proton-profiling-framework-overview). Numerical configurations and weight quantization utilities are provided in [`python/triton_kernels/bench/bench_utils.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/bench/bench_utils.py), which supports various data types, including custom mixed-precision formats.  
基准测试组件主要位于 `python/triton_kernels/bench` ，专注于评估分布式 MoE MLP 模型。这包括分析性能，尤其是在不同的量化方案下，并通过屋顶线图可视化结果。基准测试设计为在分布式环境中运行，利用优化的 Triton 内核。该组件内的关键功能包括 `bench_mlp` ，它协调单个基准测试运行，管理内存池、输入张量和精度配置。它还与 `proton` 集成以进行详细分析，并使用 `torch.cuda.CUDAGraph` 捕获和重放计算以进行稳定的性能测量。然后， `roofline_mlp` 功能整合这些基准测试以生成屋顶线图，帮助分析计算强度和内存带宽使用情况。有关 Proton 框架的更多详细信息，请参阅 Proton 分析框架概述。数值配置和权重量化工具在 `python/triton_kernels/bench/bench_utils.py` 中提供，它支持各种数据类型，包括自定义混合精度格式。

The testing framework, housed in [`python/triton_kernels/tests`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/tests), uses [`pytest`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/Makefile#L9) for orchestrating tests. It includes fixtures that configure isolated Triton environments for each test, such as [`fresh_knobs`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/test/conftest.py#L31) for resetting Triton's internal knob settings and [`fresh_triton_cache`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/test/conftest.py#L21) for managing temporary cache directories. This isolation prevents tests from interfering with each other's configurations or cached results. The tests cover a wide array of Triton kernel functionalities, including:  
测试框架位于 `python/triton_kernels/tests` 中，使用 `pytest` 来协调测试。它包含用于为每个测试配置独立 Triton 环境的固定装置，例如 `fresh_knobs` 用于重置 Triton 的内部旋钮设置，以及 `fresh_triton_cache` 用于管理临时缓存目录。这种隔离防止测试相互干扰配置或缓存结果。测试涵盖了广泛的 Triton 内核功能，包括：

-   Matrix multiplication ([`matmul`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/09-persistent-matmul.py#L162)) with diverse input shapes, data types (including mixed-precision FP8 and FP4), and architectural optimizations such as Blackwell MXScale handling, as seen in [`python/triton_kernels/tests/test_matmul.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/tests/test_matmul.py) and [`python/triton_kernels/tests/test_matmul_details`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/tests/test_matmul_details).  
    矩阵乘法（ `matmul` ）支持多样的输入形状、数据类型（包括混合精度 FP8 和 FP4），以及如 Blackwell MXScale 处理等架构优化，如 `python/triton_kernels/tests/test_matmul.py` 和 `python/triton_kernels/tests/test_matmul_details` 所示。
-   Mixed-precision floating-point (MXFP) operations, validating quantization and dequantization for various formats in [`python/triton_kernels/tests/test_mxfp.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/tests/test_mxfp.py).  
    混合精度浮点（MXFP）运算，验证 `python/triton_kernels/tests/test_mxfp.py` 中各种格式的量化与反量化。
-   Distributed expert sharding, which verifies the correctness and performance of MoE operations across multiple GPUs, including expert assignment and data distribution using [`convert_dp_to_ep`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py#L176) and [`convert_ep_to_dp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/distributed.py#L256) functions in [`python/triton_kernels/tests/test_distributed.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/tests/test_distributed.py).  
    分布式专家分片，验证 MoE 操作在多个 GPU 上的正确性与性能，包括专家分配和数据分布，使用 `convert_dp_to_ep` 和 `convert_ep_to_dp` 函数在 `python/triton_kernels/tests/test_distributed.py` 中实现。
-   Reduction operations ([`reduce`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1215)) across various dimensions and data types, including custom post-processing, as tested in [`python/triton_kernels/tests/test_reduce.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/tests/test_reduce.py).  
    跨不同维度和数据类型的归约运算（ `reduce` ），包括自定义后处理，如 `python/triton_kernels/tests/test_reduce.py` 所示。
-   Top-K selection logic ([`topk`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/topk.py#L88)), including distributed all-gather scenarios, verified in [`python/triton_kernels/tests/test_topk.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/tests/test_topk.py).  
    Top-K 选择逻辑（ `topk` ），包括分布式全收集场景，已在 `python/triton_kernels/tests/test_topk.py` 中验证。
-   SwiGLU activation functions, ensuring numerical accuracy against PyTorch references in [`python/triton_kernels/tests/test_swiglu.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/tests/test_swiglu.py).  
    SwiGLU 激活函数，在 `python/triton_kernels/tests/test_swiglu.py` 中确保了与 PyTorch 参考的数值精度。
-   Tensor metadata generation and layout transformations for ragged tensors and bitmatrices, with architecture-specific layouts for Blackwell, CDNA4, GFX1250, and Hopper architectures, as detailed in [`python/triton_kernels/tests/test_tensor.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/tests/test_tensor.py) and [`python/triton_kernels/tests/test_tensor_details`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/tests/test_tensor_details).  
    张量元数据生成和布局转换，用于不规则的张量和位矩阵，为 Blackwell、CDNA4、GFX1250 和 Hopper 架构提供特定布局，详细说明见 `python/triton_kernels/tests/test_tensor.py` 和 `python/triton_kernels/tests/test_tensor_details` 。

The framework also includes tests for kernel specialization and caching mechanisms ([`python/triton_kernels/tests/test_specialize.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/tests/test_specialize.py)), ensuring that generated Triton IR correctly includes line information for debugging. Performance measurement utilities, such as [`get_memset_tbps`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/roofline.py#L87) for memory bandwidth and [`get_blas_tflops`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/roofline.py#L135) for floating-point operations, are validated in [`python/triton_kernels/tests/test_roofline.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/tests/test_roofline.py) to ensure accurate reporting of hardware capabilities.  
该框架还包括内核特化和缓存机制的测试（ `python/triton_kernels/tests/test_specialize.py` ），确保生成的 Triton IR 正确包含行信息以用于调试。性能测量工具，如 `get_memset_tbps` 用于内存带宽和 `get_blas_tflops` 用于浮点运算，在 `python/triton_kernels/tests/test_roofline.py` 中经过验证以确保硬件能力的准确报告。

## GPU Backend Integrations  GPU 后端集成

link

zoom\_in

Triton's GPU backend integrates with different hardware platforms to enable efficient execution of compiled kernels. The architecture supports NVIDIA GPUs, managing CUDA driver interactions, applying optimizations specific to Hopper architectures, and defining NVIDIA-specific MLIR dialects. Similarly, it includes an AMD GPU backend that handles compilation to AMDGCN HSACO, kernel execution via HIP, and integration with [`hipBLASLt`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/include/hipblas-common/hipblas-common.h#L31) for GEMM operations.  
Triton 的 GPU 后端与不同的硬件平台集成，以实现编译内核的高效执行。该架构支持 NVIDIA GPU，管理 CUDA 驱动交互，应用针对 Hopper 架构的优化，并定义 NVIDIA 特定的 MLIR 方言。类似地，它还包括一个 AMD GPU 后端，该后端处理编译到 AMDGCN HSACO、通过 HIP 执行内核，以及与 `hipBLASLt` 集成以进行 GEMM 操作。

The NVIDIA GPU backend, primarily configured through [`third_party/nvidia/CMakeLists.txt`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/CMakeLists.txt), manages the multi-stage compilation pipeline from Triton's Intermediate Representation (IR) to PTX and CUBIN binaries. This involves various optimization passes as described in [Triton MLIR Transformation Passes](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#triton-compiler-architecture-triton-mlir-transformation-passes). The backend utilizes [`CUDABackend`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/backend/compiler.py#L154) within [`third_party/nvidia/backend/compiler.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/backend/compiler.py) to orchestrate this process, including code generation and GPU feature management. Low-level CUDA driver interaction is handled through Python bindings in [`third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.py) and its C extension [`third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.c`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.c), facilitating kernel loading, launching, and device management. Optimized matrix multiplication operations leveraging cuBLASLt are managed by [`CublasLtInstance`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/triton_nvidia.cc#L314) in [`third_party/nvidia/include/cublas_instance.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/include/cublas_instance.h) and exposed through Python bindings in [`third_party/nvidia/triton_nvidia.cc`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/triton_nvidia.cc).  
NVIDIA GPU 后端，主要通过 `third_party/nvidia/CMakeLists.txt` 进行配置，管理从 Triton 的中间表示（IR）到 PTX 和 CUBIN 二进制的多阶段编译流程。这涉及 Triton MLIR 转换流程中描述的各种优化过程。后端在 `third_party/nvidia/backend/compiler.py` 中使用 `CUDABackend` 来协调这一过程，包括代码生成和 GPU 功能管理。通过 `third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.py` 中的 Python 绑定及其 C 扩展 `third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.c` 处理低级 CUDA 驱动器交互，从而实现内核加载、启动和设备管理。利用 cuBLASLt 的优化矩阵乘法操作由 `third_party/nvidia/include/cublas_instance.h` 中的 `CublasLtInstance` 管理，并通过 `third_party/nvidia/triton_nvidia.cc` 中的 Python 绑定暴露。

For NVIDIA's Hopper architecture, specialized transformations are implemented in the [`third_party/nvidia/hopper`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper) directory. The [`NVGPUWarpSpecializationPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization.cpp#L27) plays a role in optimizing GPU kernel execution by performing task, data, and code partitioning, and enabling asynchronous memory operations with token-based synchronization. NVIDIA-specific MLIR dialects, such as [`NVGPU`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L4) and [`NVWS`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L5), are defined in [`third_party/nvidia/include/Dialect`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/include/Dialect) and converted to LLVM IR through passes in [`third_party/nvidia/include/NVGPUToLLVM`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/include/NVGPUToLLVM) and [`third_party/nvidia/include/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/include/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM). These conversions manage shared memory, barrier synchronization, specialized dot product, and element-wise operations. Additional CUDA language extensions for Triton programs, including [`libdevice`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/tools/build_extern.py#L148) intrinsics, Grid Dependency Control (GDC) for SM90+, and hardware access utilities, are available in [`third_party/nvidia/language`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/language). Tools for embedding, loading, linking, and executing CUDA kernels are located in [`third_party/nvidia/tools`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/tools).  
对于 NVIDIA 的 Hopper 架构，专门的转换在 `third_party/nvidia/hopper` 目录中实现。 `NVGPUWarpSpecializationPass` 通过执行任务、数据和代码分区，以及启用基于令牌同步的异步内存操作，优化 GPU 内核执行。NVIDIA 特定的 MLIR 方言，如 `NVGPU` 和 `NVWS` ，在 `third_party/nvidia/include/Dialect` 中定义，并通过 `third_party/nvidia/include/NVGPUToLLVM` 和 `third_party/nvidia/include/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM` 中的传递转换为 LLVM IR。这些转换管理共享内存、屏障同步、专门的点积和逐元素操作。Triton 程序的 CUDA 语言扩展，包括 `libdevice` 内联函数、SM90+的网格依赖控制（GDC）和硬件访问工具，在 `third_party/nvidia/language` 中提供。嵌入、加载、链接和执行 CUDA 内核的工具位于 `third_party/nvidia/tools` 。

The AMD GPU backend, configured through [`third_party/amd/CMakeLists.txt`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/CMakeLists.txt), manages the compilation pipeline from Triton IR to AMDGCN HSACO. The [`HIPBackend`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py#L111) class in [`third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py) handles the compilation and optimization stages, leading to the generation of the final HSACO binary. Interaction with the HIP runtime is facilitated by the [`HIPDriver`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/driver.py#L374) in [`third_party/amd/backend/driver.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/driver.py), which provides a Python interface for device management and kernel launching via [`hipDrvLaunchKernelEx`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/include/hip/amd_detail/hip_prof_str.h#L1731). The backend supports an [`TritonAMDGPU`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/gluon_ir.cc#L12) MLIR dialect defined in [`third_party/amd/lib/Dialect`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect), along with analysis utilities and transformation passes for optimizing dot products, pipelining, and memory operations. HIP-specific language extensions, including [`libdevice`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/tools/build_extern.py#L148) functionalities and hardware counters, are provided in [`third_party/amd/language/hip`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/language/hip). The integration with [`hipBLASLt`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/include/hipblas-common/hipblas-common.h#L31) for GEMM operations, along with optimized kernels for specific architectures like GFX1250, is available through Python bindings in [`third_party/amd/python/triton_amd.cc`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/python/triton_amd.cc).  
AMD GPU 后端，通过 `third_party/amd/CMakeLists.txt` 配置，管理从 Triton IR 到 AMDGCN HSACO 的编译流程。 `HIPBackend` 类在 `third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py` 中处理编译和优化阶段，最终生成 HSACO 二进制文件。通过与 `HIPDriver` 在 `third_party/amd/backend/driver.py` 中的交互，实现与 HIP 运行时的通信，该接口提供 Python 方式管理设备和启动内核的功能。后端支持在 `third_party/amd/lib/Dialect` 中定义的 `TritonAMDGPU` MLIR 方言，以及用于优化点积、流水线和内存操作的分析工具和转换过程。HIP 特定的语言扩展，包括 `libdevice` 功能和硬件计数器，在 `third_party/amd/language/hip` 中提供。通过 `third_party/amd/python/triton_amd.cc` 中的 Python 绑定，可以集成 `hipBLASLt` 用于 GEMM 操作，并提供针对特定架构如 GFX1250 的优化内核。

### NVIDIA GPU Backend Implementation and Compilation Pipeline  
NVIDIA GPU 后端实现与编译流程

link

zoom\_in

The NVIDIA backend within Triton's compiler architecture is responsible for translating Triton's intermediate representations into executable code for NVIDIA GPUs. This process involves a multi-stage compilation pipeline, a series of optimization passes, and the management of GPU-specific features and metadata.  
Triton 编译器架构中的 NVIDIA 后端负责将 Triton 的中间表示转换为 NVIDIA GPU 的可执行代码。这个过程涉及多阶段编译管道、一系列优化过程以及 GPU 特定特性和元数据的管理。

The compilation pipeline begins with Triton IR (TTIR) and progresses through Triton GPU IR (TTGIR) to LLVM IR before generating PTX and CUBIN binaries. This entire process is orchestrated by the [`CUDABackend`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/backend/compiler.py#L154) class defined in [`third_party/nvidia/backend/compiler.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/backend/compiler.py).  
编译流程始于 Triton IR（TTIR），然后通过 Triton GPU IR（TTGIR）进展到 LLVM IR，最终生成 PTX 和 CUBIN 二进制文件。整个流程由在 `CUDABackend` 中定义的 `third_party/nvidia/backend/compiler.py` 类进行协调。

A key aspect of this backend is the extensive use of MLIR passes to gradually lower and optimize the code. These passes are applied at different stages of the compilation:  
这一后端的关键方面是广泛使用 MLIR passes 来逐步降低和优化代码。这些 passes 在编译的不同阶段应用：

-   **TTIR stage**: Initial Triton IR undergoes canonicalization, inlining, and loop unrolling, among other transformations.  
    TTIR 阶段：初始 Triton IR 会进行规范化、内联和循环展平等其他转换。
-   **TTGIR stage**: Triton GPU IR is subject to numerous GPU-specific optimizations. These include coalescing memory accesses, optimizing dot product operations, applying Hopper architecture-specific warp specialization (discussed further in [NVIDIA Hopper Architecture Optimizations](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#gpu-backend-integrations-nvidia-hopper-architecture-optimizations)), scheduling loops, pipelining, and lowering operations for NVIDIA's Tensor Cores.  
    TTGIR 阶段：Triton GPU IR 会进行多种 GPU 特定的优化。这些包括合并内存访问、优化点积操作、应用 Hopper 架构特定的 warp 特化（将在 NVIDIA Hopper 架构优化中进一步讨论）、调度循环、流水线化以及为 NVIDIA 的 Tensor Cores 降低操作。
-   **LLVM IR stage**: The LLVM IR generation phase includes allocating shared memory and global scratch memory, converting MLIR structures to LLVM's internal representation, linking external libraries such as [`libdevice`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/tools/build_extern.py#L148), and applying further optimizations to the LLVM module.  
    LLVM IR 阶段：LLVM IR 生成阶段包括分配共享内存和全局暂存内存，将 MLIR 结构转换为 LLVM 的内部表示，链接外部库（如 `libdevice` ），并对 LLVM 模块应用进一步优化。

The backend also handles the generation of PTX assembly from LLVM IR using [`llvm.translate_to_asm`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py#L509) and then compiles this PTX into a CUBIN binary using the [`ptxas`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/knobs.py#L494) tool. This involves managing PTX versions, querying GPU features, and handling compilation parameters such as the number of warps, CTAs, and register limits via [`CUDAOptions`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/backend/compiler.py#L106). Metadata like shared memory usage and warp counts are extracted from the compiled output.  
后端还负责使用 `llvm.translate_to_asm` 从 LLVM IR 生成 PTX 汇编，然后使用 `ptxas` 工具将 PTX 编译成 CUBIN 二进制文件。这包括管理 PTX 版本、查询 GPU 特性，并通过 `CUDAOptions` 处理编译参数，如 warp 数量、CTA 数量和寄存器限制。共享内存使用和 warp 计数等元数据是从编译输出中提取的。

Interaction with the CUDA driver is managed through a Python interface to low-level CUDA functionalities, as seen in [`third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.c`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.c) and [`third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.py). This interface allows for loading and launching kernels, managing device context, and querying device properties. The [`CudaLauncher`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.py#L271) prepares and launches CUDA kernels by processing kernel metadata and arguments, including specialized handling for Tensor Memory Accelerator (TMA) descriptors for efficient data transfer on modern NVIDIA architectures. This dual approach ensures Triton can operate seamlessly within various environments, including PyTorch.  
与 CUDA 驱动器的交互通过一个 Python 接口管理低级 CUDA 功能，如 `third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.c` 和 `third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.py` 所示。该接口允许加载和启动内核、管理设备上下文以及查询设备属性。 `CudaLauncher` 通过处理内核元数据和参数来准备和启动 CUDA 内核，包括对 Tensor Memory Accelerator (TMA)描述符的专门处理，以在现代 NVIDIA 架构上进行高效数据传输。这种双重方法确保 Triton 可以在各种环境中无缝运行，包括 PyTorch。

### NVIDIA Hopper Architecture Optimizations  
NVIDIA Hopper 架构优化

link

zoom\_in

Optimizations for NVIDIA Hopper GPUs in Triton primarily leverage the [`NVGPUWarpSpecializationPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization.cpp#L27), a multi-step compilation pass that transforms Triton GPU Intermediate Representation (IR). This pass aims to enhance kernel execution efficiency by partitioning tasks, data, and code across different warp groups, managing asynchronous memory operations, and implementing token-based synchronization.  
在 Triton 中对 NVIDIA Hopper GPU 的优化主要利用了 `NVGPUWarpSpecializationPass` ，这是一个多步骤的编译过程，用于转换 Triton GPU 中间表示（IR）。此过程旨在通过在不同 warp 组之间划分任务、数据和代码，管理异步内存操作，以及实现基于令牌的同步来提高内核执行效率。

The [`NVGPUWarpSpecializationPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization.cpp#L27) is defined in [`third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization.cpp). It operates on functions within the Triton IR that are marked for warp specialization and have multiple stages, indicating pipelined execution. The pass performs the following sequence of transformations:  
`NVGPUWarpSpecializationPass` 定义在 `third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization.cpp` 中。它作用于在 Triton IR 中标记为 warp 特化的函数，这些函数具有多个阶段，表示流水线执行。该 pass 执行以下转换序列：

The initial step involves **task partitioning**, where producer-consumer relationships within the kernel, such as those between matrix multiplication operations ([`ttng::WarpGroupDotOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/gluon_ir.cc#L769), [`mlir::triton::DotOpInterface`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Dialect/Triton/IR/OpInterfaces.cpp#L38)) and memory loads ([`tt::LoadOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Dialect/TritonInstrument/Transforms/FpSanitizer.cpp#L553), [`tt::DescriptorLoadOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Dialect/TritonGPU/Transforms/Pipeliner/LowerLoops.cpp#L91)), are analyzed. This analysis assigns [`async_task_id`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/NVWS/ops.mlir#L102)s to operations, effectively separating work into distinct asynchronous tasks. This partitioning is managed by [`doTaskPartition`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization.cpp#L18) in [`third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSTaskPartition.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSTaskPartition.cpp).  
初始步骤涉及任务划分，其中分析内核内的生产者-消费者关系，例如矩阵乘法操作（ `ttng::WarpGroupDotOp` ， `mlir::triton::DotOpInterface` ）与内存加载（ `tt::LoadOp` ， `tt::DescriptorLoadOp` ）之间的关系。这种分析将 `async_task_id` 分配给操作，有效地将工作划分为不同的异步任务。这种划分由 `doTaskPartition` 在 `third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSTaskPartition.cpp` 中管理。

Following task partitioning, **task ID propagation** ensures that these [`async_task_id`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/NVWS/ops.mlir#L102)s are consistently applied throughout the function's operations. This is achieved through a sparse backward dataflow analysis that propagates task identifiers from consumers back to their producers, using [`doTaskIdPropagate`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization.cpp#L19) in [`third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSTaskIdPropagate.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSTaskIdPropagate.cpp).  
在任务划分之后，任务 ID 传播确保这些 `async_task_id` 在函数的整个操作过程中保持一致。这是通过稀疏反向数据流分析实现的，该分析使用 `doTaskIdPropagate` 在 `third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSTaskIdPropagate.cpp` 中将任务标识符从消费者传播回它们的生成者。

Next, **data partitioning** reorganizes data access patterns for multiple consuming warp groups. For operations like [`nvidia_gpu::WarpGroupDotOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Dialect/TritonGPU/Transforms/AccelerateMatmul.cpp#L427) and [`nvidia_gpu::TCGen5MMAOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Dialect/TritonGPU/Transforms/AccelerateMatmul.cpp#L590), this involves duplicating or slicing operations and their associated data to ensure each consumer group receives the necessary input efficiently. The [`doDataPartition`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization.cpp#L20) function in [`third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSDataPartition.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSDataPartition.cpp) handles this by rewriting and cloning operations while maintaining [`async_task_id`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/NVWS/ops.mlir#L102) consistency.  
接下来，数据分区会重新组织多个消费 warp 组的数据访问模式。对于 `nvidia_gpu::WarpGroupDotOp` 和 `nvidia_gpu::TCGen5MMAOp` 等操作，这涉及复制或切片操作及其相关数据，以确保每个消费者组能够高效地接收必要的输入。在 `third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSDataPartition.cpp` 中的 `doDataPartition` 函数通过重写和克隆操作来处理这个问题，同时保持 `async_task_id` 的一致性。

The **code partitioning** phase is responsible for identifying and synchronizing asynchronous data transfers. It groups related communication channels and inserts special [`CommChannel`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/CodePartitionUtility.h#L45) objects into the IR to facilitate synchronization. Token-based mechanisms are introduced using [`ttnvws::CreateTokenOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSLowerToken.cpp#L108), [`ttnvws::ProducerAcquireOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSLowerToken.cpp#L36), [`ttnvws::ProducerCommitOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSLowerToken.cpp#L62), [`ttnvws::ConsumerWaitOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSLowerToken.cpp#L36), and [`ttnvws::ConsumerReleaseOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSLowerToken.cpp#L91) to manage the flow of data and control between warp groups. Shared memory buffers are also allocated at this stage to support these asynchronous operations. This process is managed by [`doCodePartition`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization.cpp#L21) in [`third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSCodePartition.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSCodePartition.cpp).  
代码分区阶段负责识别和同步异步数据传输。它将相关的通信通道分组，并将特殊的 `CommChannel` 对象插入到中间表示（IR）中以便同步。使用 `ttnvws::CreateTokenOp` 、 `ttnvws::ProducerAcquireOp` 、 `ttnvws::ProducerCommitOp` 、 `ttnvws::ConsumerWaitOp` 和 `ttnvws::ConsumerReleaseOp` 引入基于令牌的机制来管理数据和控制流，以便在 warp 组之间进行。在这个阶段还分配了共享内存缓冲区来支持这些异步操作。此过程由 `doCodePartition` 在 `third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSCodePartition.cpp` 中管理。

Finally, **token lowering** converts these [`ttnvws`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSLowerToken.cpp#L21) dialect token operations into [`ttng`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/ir.cc#L51) barrier operations, effectively mapping the high-level synchronization primitives to lower-level barrier instructions executable on the GPU. This ensures that the specialized warp groups can coordinate their execution effectively. The [`doTokenLowering`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization.cpp#L22) function in [`third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSLowerToken.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSLowerToken.cpp) handles this translation.  
最后，token 降低将这些 `ttnvws` 方言 token 操作转换为 `ttng` 屏障操作，有效地将高级同步原语映射到可在 GPU 上执行的较低级屏障指令。这确保了专门的 warp 组能够有效协调它们的执行。 `third_party/nvidia/hopper/lib/Transforms/WarpSpecialization/WSLowerToken.cpp` 中的 `doTokenLowering` 函数处理这种转换。

These transformations are designed to optimize the use of Hopper's specialized hardware features, such as Tensor Memory Accelerator (TMA) and Warp Group Matrix Multiply-Accumulate (WGMMA) instructions, for improved performance in deep learning workloads. The overall build system and MLIR framework integration for Hopper-specific optimizations are configured in [`third_party/nvidia/hopper`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/hopper). More details on NVIDIA's MLIR dialects and their LLVM conversion can be found in [NVIDIA MLIR Dialects and LLVM Conversion](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#gpu-backend-integrations-nvidia-mlir-dialects-and-llvm-conversion).  
这些转换旨在优化 Hopper 的专用硬件功能的使用，例如 Tensor Memory Accelerator（TMA）和 Warp Group Matrix Multiply-Accumulate（WGMMA）指令，以提高深度学习工作负载的性能。针对 Hopper 的特定优化的整体构建系统和 MLIR 框架集成在 `third_party/nvidia/hopper` 中配置。有关 NVIDIA 的 MLIR 方言及其 LLVM 转换的更多详细信息，请参阅 NVIDIA MLIR 方言和 LLVM 转换。

### NVIDIA MLIR Dialects and LLVM Conversion  
NVIDIA MLIR 方言和 LLVM 转换

link

zoom\_in

Triton extends the MLIR framework with NVIDIA-specific dialects, [`NVGPU`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L4) and [`NVWS`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L5), to represent GPU-specific constructs and specialized warp-level programming paradigms. These dialects are crucial for enabling fine-grained control over NVIDIA hardware features and for optimizing performance. The build system integrates these dialects and their associated transformation passes, ensuring that Triton can effectively target NVIDIA GPUs.  
Triton 通过 NVIDIA 特定的方言 `NVGPU` 和 `NVWS` 扩展了 MLIR 框架，用于表示 GPU 特定的结构和专门的 warp 级编程范式。这些方言对于实现对 NVIDIA 硬件特性的细粒度控制以及优化性能至关重要。构建系统集成了这些方言及其相关的转换过程，确保 Triton 能够有效地针对 NVIDIA GPU。

The [`NVGPU`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L4) dialect, defined within [`third_party/nvidia/include/Dialect/NVGPU`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/include/Dialect/NVGPU), is designed to express general GPU operations within MLIR. It includes definitions for GPU-specific operations, attributes, and types. This dialect serves as an intermediate representation that bridges Triton's high-level abstractions with NVIDIA's hardware capabilities.  
`NVGPU` 方言，定义在 `third_party/nvidia/include/Dialect/NVGPU` 中，旨在表达 MLIR 中的通用 GPU 操作。它包含针对 GPU 特定操作的定义、属性和类型。该方言作为中间表示，连接了 Triton 的高级抽象与 NVIDIA 的硬件能力。

The [`NVWS`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L5) (NVIDIA Warp Specialization) dialect, located in [`third_party/nvidia/include/Dialect/NVWS`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/include/Dialect/NVWS), provides specialized constructs for managing warp-level parallelism and asynchronous memory operations on NVIDIA GPUs. It enables the compiler to orchestrate complex data movement and synchronization patterns, particularly relevant for advanced architectures like Hopper. The dialect includes operations for managing [`Aref`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/NVWS/invalid.mlir#L22) (Asynchronous Reference) objects, which facilitate producer-consumer relationships between warps, as well as [`WarpGroupOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/lib/Dialect/NVWS/IR/Ops.cpp#L109) for organizing groups of warps.  
`NVWS` （NVIDIA Warp Specialization）方言位于 `third_party/nvidia/include/Dialect/NVWS` ，为管理 NVIDIA GPU 上的 warp 级并行和异步内存操作提供了专用结构。它使编译器能够协调复杂的数据移动和同步模式，尤其适用于 Hopper 等高级架构。该方言包括用于管理 `Aref` （异步引用）对象的操作，这些操作促进了 warp 之间的生产者-消费者关系，以及用于组织 warp 组的 `WarpGroupOp` 。

A critical aspect of Triton's NVIDIA backend is the conversion of these MLIR dialects into LLVM IR and, subsequently, into PTX assembly. This process involves several conversion passes that translate [`NVGPU`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L4) and [`NVWS`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L5) operations into their corresponding LLVM/NVVM representations. For example, the [`ConvertNVGPUToLLVM`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/lib/NVGPUToLLVM/NVGPUToLLVMPass.cpp#L637) pass, defined in [`third_party/nvidia/lib/NVGPUToLLVM/NVGPUToLLVMPass.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/lib/NVGPUToLLVM/NVGPUToLLVMPass.cpp), handles the lowering of [`NVGPU`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L4) operations by generating PTX inline assembly and managing tensor memory allocation through PTX intrinsics. Similarly, the [`ConvertTritonGPUToLLVM`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/lib/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM/TritonGPUToLLVM.cpp#L82) pass, implemented in [`third_party/nvidia/lib/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM/TritonGPUToLLVM.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/lib/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM/TritonGPUToLLVM.cpp), is responsible for converting Triton GPU and Triton NVIDIA GPU dialects into LLVM/NVVM IR, taking into account the target GPU's compute capability and PTX version.  
Triton 的 NVIDIA 后端的一个关键方面是将这些 MLIR 方言转换为 LLVM IR，并进一步转换为 PTX 汇编。此过程涉及多个转换过程，这些过程将 `NVGPU` 和 `NVWS` 操作转换为相应的 LLVM/NVVM 表示。例如，定义在 `third_party/nvidia/lib/NVGPUToLLVM/NVGPUToLLVMPass.cpp` 中的 `ConvertNVGPUToLLVM` 过程处理 `NVGPU` 操作的降级，通过生成 PTX 内联汇编和管理通过 PTX 内联函数进行的张量内存分配。类似地，在 `third_party/nvidia/lib/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM/TritonGPUToLLVM.cpp` 中实现的 `ConvertTritonGPUToLLVM` 过程负责将 Triton GPU 和 Triton NVIDIA GPU 方言转换为 LLVM/NVVM IR，同时考虑目标 GPU 的计算能力和 PTX 版本。

This conversion pipeline includes specialized lowering strategies for various operations:  
这个转换流程包括针对各种操作的专门优化策略：

-   **Shared Memory Management**: Passes like [`createAllocateSharedMemoryNvPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/include/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM/Passes.h#L26) in [`third_party/nvidia/include/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM/Passes.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/include/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM/Passes.h) manage the allocation and optimization of shared memory.  
    共享内存管理：像 `createAllocateSharedMemoryNvPass` 这样的 pass 负责管理共享内存的分配和优化。
-   **Barrier Synchronization**: The compiler converts high-level barrier operations and cluster launch control primitives into low-level LLVM/NVVM intrinsics or inline PTX to ensure correct synchronization across warps and thread blocks. This is particularly important for architectures with advanced synchronization features.  
    屏障同步：编译器将高级屏障操作和集群启动控制原语转换为低级的 LLVM/NVVM 内联函数或 PTX 内联代码，以确保跨 warp 和线程块的正确同步。这对于具有高级同步功能的架构尤为重要。
-   **Warp Specialization**: The [`ConvertWarpSpecializeToLLVM`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/lib/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM/ConvertWarpSpecializeToLLVM.cpp#L253) pass transforms warp specialization constructs into NVIDIA-specific LLVM IR, often involving adjustments to register allocation and the use of NVIDIA-specific barrier intrinsics.  
    warp 特化： `ConvertWarpSpecializeToLLVM` pass 将 warp 特化结构转换为 NVIDIA 特定的 LLVM IR，通常涉及寄存器分配的调整和使用 NVIDIA 特定的屏障内联函数。
-   **Dot Product Operations**: Triton employs highly optimized lowering for matrix multiplication operations ([`triton::DotOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Analysis/Utility.cpp#L1163)). This involves translating them into specialized hardware instructions like MMAv2, MMAv5 (using [`tcgen05`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/Conversion/nvgpu_to_llvm.mlir#L82) PTX), and WGMMA, leveraging Tensor Cores for efficient computation.  
    点积运算：Triton 对矩阵乘法运算（ `triton::DotOp` ）采用高度优化的降低（lowering）。这涉及将它们转换为特殊的硬件指令，如 MMAv2、MMAv5（使用 `tcgen05` PTX）和 WGMMA，并利用 Tensor Cores 进行高效计算。
-   **Element-wise and Memory Operations**: Conversions handle element-wise operations, including mixed-precision floating-point arithmetic (e.g., FP8, BF16, FP16), and memory operations such as loads, stores, atomics, and asynchronous copies ([`cp.async`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/Conversion/tma_to_llvm.mlir#L68)). The Tensor Memory Accelerator (TMA) operations, such as [`TensormapCreateOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Dialect/TritonNvidiaGPU/IR/Ops.cpp#L1205) and [`TensormapFenceproxyAcquireOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Dialect/TritonNvidiaGPU/Transforms/TMALowering.cpp#L175), are also translated into PTX for descriptor manipulation and fence operations.  
    逐元素和内存操作：转换处理逐元素操作，包括混合精度浮点数运算（例如，FP8、BF16、FP16），以及加载、存储、原子操作和异步复制等内存操作（ `cp.async` ）。Tensor 内存加速器（TMA）操作，如 `TensormapCreateOp` 和 `TensormapFenceproxyAcquireOp` ，也转换为 PTX 用于描述符操作和栅栏操作。

The generation of PTX assembly strings is a recurring theme, with [`PTXBuilder`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Conversion/TritonInstrumentToLLVM/InstrumentationToLLVM.cpp#L191) (defined in [`third_party/nvidia/include/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM/PTXAsmFormat.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/include/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM/PTXAsmFormat.h)) providing an API to programmatically construct PTX code for [`llvm.inline_asm`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/TritonGPU/atomic-cas.mlir#L3) operations. This allows for fine-tuned control over the generated machine code, which is essential for maximizing GPU performance. The [`CublasLtInstance`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/triton_nvidia.cc#L314) class, found in [`third_party/nvidia/include/cublas_instance.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/include/cublas_instance.h), further enhances this by integrating with the [`cuBLASLt`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/include/cublas_instance.h#L348) library for highly optimized GEMM operations, handling dynamic library loading and efficient algorithm selection.  
PTX 汇编字符串的生成是一个反复出现的主题， `PTXBuilder` （定义在 `third_party/nvidia/include/TritonNVIDIAGPUToLLVM/PTXAsmFormat.h` 中）提供了一个 API 来编程构造用于 `llvm.inline_asm` 操作的 PTX 代码。这允许对生成的机器代码进行精细控制，这对于最大化 GPU 性能至关重要。在 `third_party/nvidia/include/cublas_instance.h` 中找到的 `CublasLtInstance` 类，通过与 `cuBLASLt` 库集成，进一步增强了这一点，用于高度优化的 GEMM 操作，处理动态库加载和高效算法选择。

### NVIDIA CUDA Language Extensions and Tools  
NVIDIA CUDA 语言扩展和工具

link

zoom\_in

Triton provides a set of CUDA-specific functionalities that can be invoked directly from Triton programs, enabling fine-grained control over NVIDIA GPUs. These functionalities are exposed through a Python interface, primarily organized within the [`third_party/nvidia/language`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/language) directory.  
Triton 提供了一套 CUDA 特定的功能，可以直接从 Triton 程序中调用，从而实现对 NVIDIA GPU 的细粒度控制。这些功能通过 Python 接口暴露，主要组织在 `third_party/nvidia/language` 目录中。

A core component is the integration of NVIDIA's [`libdevice`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/tools/build_extern.py#L148) intrinsics, found in [`third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/libdevice.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/libdevice.py). This allows Triton programs to directly access a wide array of GPU-specific operations, including bit manipulation (e.g., [`clz`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/extra/libdevice.py#L1), [`popc`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/extra/libdevice.py#L5)), various integer and floating-point arithmetic functions with different rounding modes (e.g., [`fma_rn`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/extra/libdevice.py#L61), [`div_rn`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/math.py#L206)), and transcendental functions (e.g., [`exp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1194), [`log`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1197), [`sin`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/core.py#L1203)). These intrinsics are made available as external functions callable within Triton kernels, enabling optimization for native GPU capabilities.  
一个核心组件是集成 NVIDIA 的 `libdevice` 内联函数，这些内联函数位于 `third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/libdevice.py` 中。这使得 Triton 程序能够直接访问各种 GPU 特定的操作，包括位操作（例如 `clz` 、 `popc` ）、各种整数和浮点数运算函数（具有不同的舍入模式，例如 `fma_rn` 、 `div_rn` ）以及超越函数（例如 `exp` 、 `log` 、 `sin` ）。这些内联函数作为外部函数提供，可以在 Triton 内核中调用，从而实现对原生 GPU 功能的优化。

For advanced control over kernel execution, especially on newer NVIDIA architectures like SM90+, Triton incorporates Grid Dependency Control (GDC). Defined in [`third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/gdc.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/gdc.py), [`gdc_wait`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/gdc.py#L13) allows a kernel to block until preceding dependent operations complete, ensuring memory visibility. Conversely, [`gdc_launch_dependents`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/gdc.py#L28) signals the runtime to initiate subsequent dependent kernels, facilitating programmatic orchestration of kernel launches. Both functions leverage inline PTX assembly to directly interact with the GPU's grid management hardware.  
为了对内核执行进行高级控制，特别是在较新的 NVIDIA 架构如 SM90+上，Triton 集成了网格依赖控制（GDC）。在 `third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/gdc.py` 中定义， `gdc_wait` 允许内核阻塞，直到先前的依赖操作完成，确保内存可见性。相反， `gdc_launch_dependents` 向运行时发出信号，以启动后续的依赖内核，从而促进内核启动的程序化编排。这两个功能都利用内联 PTX 汇编直接与 GPU 的网格管理硬件交互。

Triton also offers utilities for accessing hardware information and performing specialized data conversions, located in [`third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/utils.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/utils.py). These include functions like [`globaltimer`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/utils.py#L5) to retrieve the GPU's 64-bit global timer and [`smid`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/language/hip/utils.py#L30) to identify the Streaming Multiprocessor ID. Additionally, the framework provides custom 8-bit floating-point conversion routines, such as [`convert_custom_float8_sm70`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/utils.py#L108) and [`convert_custom_float8_sm80`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/utils.py#L103), optimized for specific NVIDIA architectures (SM70 and SM80, respectively). These conversions are crucial for supporting mixed-precision computation in deep learning workloads.  
Triton 还提供了用于访问硬件信息和执行特殊数据转换的工具，位于 `third_party/nvidia/language/cuda/utils.py` 。这些工具包括 `globaltimer` 用于获取 GPU 的 64 位全局计时器和 `smid` 用于识别流式多处理器 ID 的函数。此外，该框架还提供了针对特定 NVIDIA 架构（分别为 SM70 和 SM80）优化的自定义 8 位浮点数转换例程，如 `convert_custom_float8_sm70` 和 `convert_custom_float8_sm80` 。这些转换对于在深度学习工作负载中支持混合精度计算至关重要。

Beyond language extensions, Triton includes tools for managing the lifecycle of compiled CUDA kernels. The [`third_party/nvidia/tools/cuda`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/tools/cuda) directory contains components for embedding, loading, linking, and executing CUDA kernels. For instance, [`third_party/nvidia/tools/cuda/compile.c`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/tools/cuda/compile.c) embeds the compiled kernel's binary data (CUBIN) directly into source code, which can then be dynamically loaded into a [`CUmodule`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.c#L250) at runtime using [`cuModuleLoadData`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/backend/driver.c#L265). This allows Triton to generate self-contained C source files that can load, configure dynamic shared memory, and launch kernels via the CUDA driver API. The [`third_party/nvidia/tools/cuda/compile.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/tools/cuda/compile.h) and [`third_party/nvidia/tools/cuda/link.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/nvidia/tools/cuda/link.h) files define the necessary C/CUDA interfaces, type aliases, and error handling mechanisms to support this kernel management process.  
除了语言扩展之外，Triton 还包含管理编译后 CUDA 内核生命周期的工具。 `third_party/nvidia/tools/cuda` 目录包含用于嵌入、加载、链接和执行 CUDA 内核的组件。例如， `third_party/nvidia/tools/cuda/compile.c` 将编译后的内核的二进制数据（CUBIN）直接嵌入到源代码中，然后可以使用 `cuModuleLoadData` 在运行时动态加载到 `CUmodule` 中。这使得 Triton 能够生成自包含的 C 源文件，这些文件可以加载、配置动态共享内存，并通过 CUDA 驱动程序 API 启动内核。 `third_party/nvidia/tools/cuda/compile.h` 和 `third_party/nvidia/tools/cuda/link.h` 文件定义了必要的 C/CUDA 接口、类型别名和错误处理机制，以支持这个内核管理过程。

For a broader understanding of how these NVIDIA-specific components integrate into the overall compilation process, refer to [NVIDIA GPU Backend Implementation and Compilation Pipeline](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#gpu-backend-integrations-nvidia-gpu-backend-implementation-and-compilation-pipeline).  
若要更全面地了解这些 NVIDIA 特定组件如何集成到整体编译过程中，请参阅 NVIDIA GPU 后端实现与编译流程。

### AMD GPU Backend Implementation and Compilation Pipeline  
AMD GPU 后端实现与编译流程

link

zoom\_in

Triton's core AMD GPU backend translates high-level Triton Intermediate Representation (IR) into executable code for AMD GPUs, specifically HSACO (HSA Code Object). This involves a multi-stage compilation pipeline, various optimization passes, and flexible configuration options through [`HIPOptions`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py#L40). The overall infrastructure for the AMD backend is found in the directory [`third_party/amd`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd).  
Triton 的核心 AMD GPU 后端将高级 Triton 中间表示（IR）转换为 AMD GPU 的可执行代码，具体为 HSACO（HSA 代码对象）。这涉及多阶段编译流程、多种优化过程以及通过 `HIPOptions` 提供的灵活配置选项。AMD 后端的整体基础设施位于目录 `third_party/amd` 中。

The compilation pipeline is managed by the [`HIPBackend`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py#L111) class in [`third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py). It orchestrates the conversion of Triton IR through different internal representations: Triton IR (TTIR), TritonGPU IR (TTGIR), LLVM IR, and AMDGCN assembly, ultimately producing HSACO. This modular approach allows for targeted optimizations at each stage. For example, [`add_convert_to_ttgpuir`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/passes.cc#L51) converts Triton IR to TritonGPU IR, and [`add_to_llvmir`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py#L344) lowers TritonGPU IR to LLVM IR. The pipeline also integrates passes like [`add_accelerate_matmul`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/passes.cc#L72) for optimizing matrix multiplication and [`add_pipeline`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/passes.cc#L68) for loop pipelining, which can be configured for features like asynchronous copies and ping-pong scheduling.  
编译流程由 `HIPBackend` 中的 `third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py` 类管理。它协调将 Triton IR 转换为不同的内部表示形式：Triton IR (TTIR)、TritonGPU IR (TTGIR)、LLVM IR 和 AMDGCN 汇编，最终生成 HSACO。这种模块化方法允许在每个阶段进行针对性优化。例如， `add_convert_to_ttgpuir` 将 Triton IR 转换为 TritonGPU IR，而 `add_to_llvmir` 将 TritonGPU IR 降低为 LLVM IR。该流程还集成了 `add_accelerate_matmul` 用于优化矩阵乘法和 `add_pipeline` 用于循环流水线，这些功能可以配置异步拷贝和乒乓调度等特性。

Configuration options are encapsulated within the [`HIPOptions`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py#L40) dataclass, also defined in [`third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py). These options allow control over parameters such as [`num_warps`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/knobs.py#L437), [`num_stages`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/knobs.py#L439), and the target GPU [`arch`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/backends/compiler.py#L13). The [`parse_options`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/compiler/compiler.py#L83) method handles default values, architecture-specific adjustments (e.g., enabling TF32 for [`gfx942`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/TritonGPU/combine.mlir#L3741) architectures), and validation. This ensures that the compilation process is tailored to the specific AMD GPU architecture and desired performance characteristics.  
配置选项封装在 `HIPOptions` 数据类中，该数据类也在 `third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py` 中定义。这些选项允许控制 `num_warps` 、 `num_stages` 以及目标 GPU `arch` 等参数。 `parse_options` 方法处理默认值、特定架构的调整（例如，为 `gfx942` 架构启用 TF32），以及验证。这确保了编译过程针对特定的 AMD GPU 架构和期望的性能特征进行了定制。

After the MLIR passes generate LLVM IR, it is translated into AMDGCN assembly. The final step, [`make_hsaco`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py#L517), assembles this AMDGCN assembly into the executable HSACO binary using utilities from the Python bindings found in [`third_party/amd/python/triton_amd.cc`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/python/triton_amd.cc). The interaction with the HIP runtime for loading and launching these compiled kernels is handled by Python interfaces and low-level C utilities described in [AMD HIP Runtime Interaction and API](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#gpu-backend-integrations-amd-hip-runtime-interaction-and-api).  
在 MLIR passes 生成 LLVM IR 之后，它会被翻译成 AMDGCN 汇编代码。最后一步， `make_hsaco` ，使用在 `third_party/amd/python/triton_amd.cc` 中找到的 Python 绑定中的工具，将 AMDGCN 汇编代码汇编成可执行的 HSACO 二进制文件。与 HIP 运行时交互以加载和启动这些编译好的内核，由 AMD HIP 运行时交互和 API 中描述的 Python 接口和底层 C 工具处理。

The AMD GPU backend also integrates several MLIR dialects, analyses, and transformations, defined in [`third_party/amd/include`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/include) and [`third_party/amd/lib`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib). These include the [`TritonAMDGPU`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/gluon_ir.cc#L12) MLIR dialect for AMD-specific operations, analysis utilities for memory allocation and range analysis, and passes for optimizing dot products, pipelining, and memory operations. For more details on these, refer to [AMD MLIR Dialect, Analysis, and Transformations](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#gpu-backend-integrations-amd-mlir-dialect-analysis-and-transformations). The compilation process also leverages dynamic loading of [`libamdhip64.so`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/roofline.py#L100) for runtime interaction, as elaborated in [AMD HIP Language Extensions and Utilities](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#gpu-backend-integrations-amd-hip-language-extensions-and-utilities).  
AMD GPU 后端还集成了多个 MLIR 方言、分析和转换，这些内容定义在 `third_party/amd/include` 和 `third_party/amd/lib` 中。其中包括用于 AMD 特定操作的 `TritonAMDGPU` MLIR 方言、内存分配和范围分析的分析工具，以及用于优化点积、流水线和内存操作的转换。有关这些的更多详细信息，请参阅 AMD MLIR 方言、分析和转换。编译过程还利用了 `libamdhip64.so` 的动态加载以实现运行时交互，具体内容详见 AMD HIP 语言扩展和工具。

### AMD HIP Runtime Interaction and API  
AMD HIP 运行时交互与 API

link

zoom\_in
