Triton's interaction with AMD GPUs is managed through a HIP (Heterogeneous-compute Interface for Portability) backend, which handles everything from dynamic library loading to kernel execution and argument processing. This backend establishes the necessary plumbing for Triton programs to run on AMD hardware.  
Triton 与 AMD GPU 的交互通过 HIP（异构计算接口，用于可移植性）后端进行管理，该后端处理从动态库加载到内核执行和参数处理的一切事务。这个后端为 Triton 程序在 AMD 硬件上运行建立了必要的管道。

A Python-based [`HIPDriver`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/driver.py#L374) class in [`third_party/amd/backend/driver.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/driver.py) orchestrates the connection to the AMD GPU runtime. This driver is responsible for locating the [`libamdhip64.so`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/roofline.py#L100) library, which contains the core HIP API, ensuring that Triton can find and interact with the installed AMD ROCm stack. This dynamic loading mechanism allows for flexibility across different system configurations. Once the library is located, a C extension, [`third_party/amd/backend/driver.c`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/driver.c), is compiled and loaded to provide direct, low-level access to the HIP runtime. This C extension is crucial for performance-sensitive operations, translating Python calls into direct HIP API invocations.  
一个基于 Python 的 `HIPDriver` 类在 `third_party/amd/backend/driver.py` 中负责管理与 AMD GPU 运行时的连接。该驱动程序负责定位 `libamdhip64.so` 库，该库包含核心 HIP API，确保 Triton 能够找到并与已安装的 AMD ROCm 堆栈交互。这种动态加载机制允许在不同系统配置中提供灵活性。一旦定位到库，就会编译并加载 C 扩展 `third_party/amd/backend/driver.c` ，以提供对 HIP 运行时的直接、低级访问。这个 C 扩展对于性能敏感的操作至关重要，它将 Python 调用转换为直接的 HIP API 调用。

The [`HIPUtils`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/driver.py#L165) singleton class, which wraps the C extension, offers functionalities such as loading compiled kernel binaries onto the device, unloading modules, and querying device properties. For kernel launches, the [`HIPLauncher`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/driver.py#L315) class prepares and executes the kernels. It handles the intricate process of mapping Python arguments to the C-level kernel parameters, including specialized handling for Triton's Tensor Data Movement (TDM) descriptors, which are used to optimize tensor argument passing and memory access patterns. This allows Triton programs to efficiently pass complex data structures to the GPU kernels.  
`HIPUtils` 单例类，它封装了 C 扩展，提供了加载编译好的内核二进制文件到设备、卸载模块以及查询设备属性等功能。对于内核启动， `HIPLauncher` 类负责准备和执行内核。它处理将 Python 参数映射到 C 级内核参数的复杂过程，包括对 Triton 的 Tensor 数据移动（TDM）描述符的专门处理，这些描述符用于优化张量参数传递和内存访问模式。这使得 Triton 程序能够高效地将复杂的数据结构传递给 GPU 内核。

The low-level C implementation in [`third_party/amd/backend/driver.c`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/driver.c) includes an [`initSymbolTable`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/driver.c#L341) function that dynamically resolves HIP API function pointers, ensuring that all subsequent HIP calls are directed to the correct addresses within the loaded [`libamdhip64.so`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton_kernels/triton_kernels/roofline.py#L100). This file also contains mechanisms for encoding [`TDMDescriptor`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUToLLVM/TDMUtility.h#L13) objects, facilitating the detailed description of tensor layouts and access patterns for the GPU. The [`launchKernel`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/include/Runtime/Runtime.h#L18) function is central to dispatching kernels, taking care of argument extraction and mapping Python data types to their C equivalents before invoking the appropriate HIP kernel launch API. Error checking is robust, converting HIP runtime errors into Python exceptions for easier debugging.  
`third_party/amd/backend/driver.c` 中的底层 C 实现包含一个 `initSymbolTable` 函数，用于动态解析 HIP API 函数指针，确保所有后续的 HIP 调用都指向加载的 `libamdhip64.so` 内的正确地址。该文件还包含编码 `TDMDescriptor` 对象的机制，便于详细描述 GPU 的张量布局和访问模式。 `launchKernel` 函数是内核调度的核心，负责参数提取并将 Python 数据类型映射到它们的 C 对应类型，然后调用适当的 HIP 内核启动 API。错误检查功能强大，将 HIP 运行时错误转换为 Python 异常，以便于调试。

This layered approach, combining a Python interface for high-level management with low-level C utilities for direct hardware interaction, enables Triton to effectively compile and execute high-performance kernels on AMD GPUs.  
这种分层方法结合了用于高层管理的 Python 接口和用于直接硬件交互的低级 C 工具，使 Triton 能够有效地在 AMD GPU 上编译和执行高性能内核。

### AMD MLIR Dialect, Analysis, and Transformations  
AMD MLIR 方言、分析与转换

link

zoom\_in

The [`TritonAMDGPU`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/gluon_ir.cc#L12) MLIR dialect provides the foundation for compiling Triton programs to run on AMD GPUs, extending the core MLIR framework with AMD-specific operations and types. This dialect is crucial for representing GPU-specific constructs and enabling targeted optimizations for AMD architectures. Defined within [`third_party/amd/include/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/include/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR) and implemented in [`third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp), it includes operations for tensor manipulation such as [`ExtractSliceOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp#L97) for extracting tensor segments, [`ConcatOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp#L517) for combining tensors, and [`InThreadTransposeOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp#L355) for transposing 2D data within a thread. It also introduces specialized type conversion operations like [`UpcastMXFPOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp#L243), [`ScaledUpcastFp4Op`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp#L427), and [`ScaledUpcastFp8Op`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp#L507) to manage mixed-precision data types. Memory operations are a significant part of this dialect, including [`BufferLoadToLocalOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp#L623) for loading data into local memory and a suite of asynchronous TDM (Tiled Data Movement) operations like [`AsyncTDMCopyGlobalToLocalOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp#L708) and [`AsyncTDMScatterOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp#L814) for efficient data movement between global and local memory. Synchronization is handled through operations like [`InitBarrierOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/gluon_ir.cc#L837), [`WaitBarrierOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/gluon_ir.cc#L850), [`ArriveBarrierOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/gluon_ir.cc#L854), and [`ClusterBarrierArriveOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp#L1002) for managing barrier synchronization within and across compute units.  
`TritonAMDGPU` MLIR 方言为编译 Triton 程序以在 AMD GPU 上运行提供了基础，通过引入 AMD 特定的操作和类型扩展了核心 MLIR 框架。这个方言对于表示特定于 GPU 的构造以及为 AMD 架构实现定向优化至关重要。它定义在 `third_party/amd/include/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR` 中并在 `third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp` 中实现，包含了用于张量操作的运算符，例如 `ExtractSliceOp` 用于提取张量片段、 `ConcatOp` 用于合并张量以及 `InThreadTransposeOp` 用于在线程内转置 2D 数据。它还引入了专门的数据类型转换运算符，如 `UpcastMXFPOp` 、 `ScaledUpcastFp4Op` 和 `ScaledUpcastFp8Op` ，用于管理混合精度数据类型。内存操作是这个方言的重要组成部分，包括 `BufferLoadToLocalOp` 用于将数据加载到本地内存，以及一系列异步 TDM（Tiled Data Movement）操作，如 `AsyncTDMCopyGlobalToLocalOp` 和 `AsyncTDMScatterOp` ，用于在全局和本地内存之间高效地移动数据。同步通过如 `InitBarrierOp` 、 `WaitBarrierOp` 、 `ArriveBarrierOp` 和 `ClusterBarrierArriveOp` 等操作来处理，用于管理和跨计算单元的屏障同步。

Alongside the dialect, a suite of AMD-specific analysis utilities supports the compiler's optimization efforts. Memory allocation analysis, implemented in [`third_party/amd/lib/Analysis/AMDGPUAllocation.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Analysis/AMDGPUAllocation.cpp), helps determine the scratch memory requirements for operations such as layout conversions and warp specialization. This is vital for efficient shared memory utilization. Integer range analysis, detailed in [`third_party/amd/lib/Analysis/RangeAnalysis.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Analysis/RangeAnalysis.cpp), enhances the compiler's understanding of integer value ranges, leveraging assumptions ([`tl.assume`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/TritonGPU/amd/amd-range-analysis.mlir#L1731)) and loop trip counts to refine analysis for Triton-specific operations like [`GetProgramIdOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/ir.cc#L1640) and [`MakeRangeOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/ir.cc#L1158). An extension to [`AxisInfo`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Analysis/AxisInfo.cpp#L1300) analysis, found in [`third_party/amd/lib/Analysis/AxisInfoExt.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Analysis/AxisInfoExt.cpp), ensures that axis-related metadata propagates correctly through AMD-specific operations, particularly for [`ExtractSliceOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp#L97).  
除了方言之外，一套针对 AMD 的特定分析工具支持编译器的优化工作。内存分配分析，在 `third_party/amd/lib/Analysis/AMDGPUAllocation.cpp` 中实现，有助于确定诸如布局转换和 warp 特殊化等操作的临时内存需求。这对于高效利用共享内存至关重要。整数范围分析，在 `third_party/amd/lib/Analysis/RangeAnalysis.cpp` 中详细说明，通过利用假设（ `tl.assume` ）和循环迭代次数，增强了编译器对整数值范围的理解，从而优化针对 Triton 特定操作如 `GetProgramIdOp` 和 `MakeRangeOp` 的分析。在 `AxisInfo` 分析的基础上扩展的 `third_party/amd/lib/Analysis/AxisInfoExt.cpp` ，确保与轴相关的元数据能够通过 AMD 特定操作正确传播，特别是在 `ExtractSliceOp` 的情况下。

Various MLIR transformation passes are then applied to optimize code for AMD GPUs. These passes convert generic Triton IR into AMD-specific instructions and apply hardware-aware optimizations. Notable transformations include those for accelerating matrix multiplication, which convert [`DotOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/ir.cc#L1652) into highly optimized MFMA (Matrix Fused Multiply-Add), WMMA (Wave Matrix Multiply Accumulate), or FMA (Fused Multiply-Add) intrinsics as implemented in [`third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUTransforms/AccelerateAMDMatmul.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUTransforms/AccelerateAMDMatmul.cpp). Loop-level optimizations are also performed, including [`PipelinePass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Dialect/TritonGPU/Transforms/Pipeliner/SoftwarePipeliner.cpp#L171) for software pipelining and [`Pingponger`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUTransforms/BlockPingpong.cpp#L38) for scheduling, as seen in [`third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUTransforms/BlockPingpong.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUTransforms/BlockPingpong.cpp). Memory operations are further refined by passes like [`TritonAMDGPUConvertToBufferOpsPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUTransforms/ConvertToBufferOps.cpp#L590) to convert generic memory operations to AMDGPU buffer operations and [`TritonAMDGPUCoalesceAsyncCopyPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUTransforms/CoalesceAsyncCopy.cpp#L236) to optimize asynchronous copy writes. Layout transformation passes, such as [`TritonAMDGPUHoistLayoutConversionsPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUTransforms/HoistLayoutConversions.cpp#L42) and [`TritonAMDGPUInThreadTranspose`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/include/TritonAMDGPUTransforms/Passes.td#L216), ensure data layouts are optimized for memory access patterns. Finally, these MLIR dialects are converted to LLVM IR and GCN assembly, as described in [MLIR to LLVM IR Conversion and Code Generation](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#triton-compiler-architecture-mlir-to-llvm-ir-conversion-and-code-generation), with specific patterns for [`ConcatOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp#L517), [`ExtractSliceOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/Dialect/TritonAMDGPU/IR/Dialect.cpp#L97), and scaled upcast operations found in [`third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUDialectToLLVM`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUDialectToLLVM).  
随后将应用多种 MLIR 转换过程来优化 AMD GPU 的代码。这些过程将通用 Triton IR 转换为 AMD 特定的指令，并应用与硬件相关的优化。值得注意的转换包括用于加速矩阵乘法的转换，这些转换将 `DotOp` 转换为高度优化的 MFMA（Matrix Fused Multiply-Add）、WMMA（Wave Matrix Multiply Accumulate）或 FMA（Fused Multiply-Add）内联函数，如 `third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUTransforms/AccelerateAMDMatmul.cpp` 中所示。还执行了循环级优化，包括 `PipelinePass` 用于软件流水线化，以及 `Pingponger` 用于调度，如 `third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUTransforms/BlockPingpong.cpp` 所示。通过像 `TritonAMDGPUConvertToBufferOpsPass` 这样的过程进一步细化内存操作，将通用内存操作转换为 AMDGPU 缓冲区操作，以及通过 `TritonAMDGPUCoalesceAsyncCopyPass` 优化异步复制写入。布局转换过程，如 `TritonAMDGPUHoistLayoutConversionsPass` 和 `TritonAMDGPUInThreadTranspose` ，确保数据布局针对内存访问模式进行了优化。最后，这些 MLIR 方言被转换为 LLVM IR 和 GCN 汇编，如 MLIR 到 LLVM IR 转换和代码生成中所述，其中包含针对 `ConcatOp` 、 `ExtractSliceOp` 以及 `third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUDialectToLLVM` 中发现的缩放上提升操作的特定模式。

### AMD HIP Language Extensions and Utilities  
AMD HIP 语言扩展和工具

link

zoom\_in

Triton's support for AMD GPUs includes a set of language extensions and utility functions that expose HIP-specific functionalities and hardware interactions to Triton programs. These extensions allow kernels to leverage optimized math operations and access low-level hardware counters and identifiers.  
Triton 对 AMD GPU 的支持包括一组语言扩展和实用函数，这些扩展将 HIP 特定的功能和硬件交互暴露给 Triton 程序。这些扩展允许内核利用优化的数学运算，并访问低级硬件计数器和标识符。

The primary set of HIP-specific [`libdevice`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/tools/build_extern.py#L148) functionalities are exposed through external functions that wrap AMD HIP [`libdevice`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/tools/build_extern.py#L148) math operations. These functions, defined in [`third_party/amd/language/hip/libdevice.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/language/hip/libdevice.py), provide common element-wise mathematical functions such as absolute value, floor, exponential, sine, cosine, and power. They also include predicates like [`isnan`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/extra/libdevice.py#L533) and [`isinf`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/language/extra/libdevice.py#L549). The design allows Triton kernels to map these operations to their corresponding, highly optimized HIP C-style intrinsics, ensuring type safety and efficient execution on AMD GPUs.  
HIP 特定的 `libdevice` 功能主要通过外部函数暴露，这些函数封装了 AMD HIP `libdevice` 数学运算。这些函数定义在 `third_party/amd/language/hip/libdevice.py` 中，提供了常见的逐元素数学函数，如绝对值、向下取整、指数、正弦、余弦和幂运算。它们还包括 `isnan` 和 `isinf` 等谓词。该设计允许 Triton 内核将这些操作映射到相应的、高度优化的 HIP C 风格内联函数，确保在 AMD GPU 上执行时的类型安全和高效性。

In addition to mathematical operations, Triton provides utility functions for accessing AMD GPU-specific hardware information. These utilities, found in [`third_party/amd/language/hip/utils.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/language/hip/utils.py), include [`memrealtime`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/language/hip/utils.py#L5) for retrieving a 64-bit real-time counter from the hardware. This function uses inline assembly to interact directly with architecture-dependent instructions. Another key utility is [`smid`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/language/hip/utils.py#L30), which provides the compute unit or workgroup processor ID of the current wave. Its implementation is tailored to different AMD GPU architectures ([`gfx9`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/Conversion/amd/warp_id_to_llvm.mlir#L1), [`gfx10`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/language/hip/utils.py#L48), [`gfx11`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/_internal_testing.py#L87), [`gfx12`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/_internal_testing.py#L92)) to read the appropriate hardware registers. Functions like [`num_threads`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/language/hip/utils.py#L65) and [`num_warps`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/knobs.py#L437) are also provided, enabling kernels to dynamically determine the total number of threads and warps, respectively, by embedding these values as compile-time constants. The aggregation of these utilities and [`libdevice`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/tools/build_extern.py#L148) functions is handled by [`third_party/amd/language/hip/__init__.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/language/hip/__init__.py).  
除了数学运算外，Triton 还提供了用于访问 AMD GPU 特定硬件信息的实用函数。这些实用函数位于 `third_party/amd/language/hip/utils.py` 中，包括 `memrealtime` 用于从硬件获取 64 位实时计数器。该函数使用内联汇编直接与架构相关的指令交互。另一个关键实用函数是 `smid` ，它提供当前波次的计算单元或工作组处理器 ID。其实现针对不同的 AMD GPU 架构（ `gfx9` 、 `gfx10` 、 `gfx11` 、 `gfx12` ）进行了定制，以读取相应的硬件寄存器。还提供了像 `num_threads` 和 `num_warps` 这样的函数，使内核能够通过将这些值嵌入为编译时常量来动态确定线程总数和 WARP 数。这些实用函数和 `libdevice` 函数的聚合由 `third_party/amd/language/hip/__init__.py` 处理。

## Compiler Extension and Plugin System  
编译器扩展和插件系统

link

zoom\_in

Triton provides a plugin system for extending its compilation capabilities beyond default offerings, allowing for out-of-tree customization of its MLIR TTIR (Triton IR) and TTGIR (Triton GPU IR) stages. This system enables dynamic loading of custom MLIR dialects, operations, types, and transformation passes, thereby allowing users to modify or introduce new compilation behaviors without recompiling the main Triton codebase. The primary use cases for this plugin system include defining new operations and their lowering rules, implementing specialized optimizations, and inserting passes for profiling or code analysis, even for specific kernels or models.  
Triton 提供了一个插件系统，用于扩展其编译能力，超越默认功能，允许对 MLIR TTIR（Triton IR）和 TTGIR（Triton GPU IR）阶段进行树外定制。该系统支持动态加载自定义的 MLIR 方言、操作、类型和转换过程，从而使用户能够在不重新编译主 Triton 代码库的情况下修改或引入新的编译行为。该插件系统的主要用例包括定义新操作及其降低规则、实现专用优化，以及为分析或代码分析插入过程，甚至针对特定内核或模型。

The plugin system operates by loading shared libraries at runtime, which can be specified via the [`TRITON_PASS_PLUGIN_PATH`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/Makefile#L42) environment variable. Within Python, the [`knobs.runtime.add_stages_inspection_hook`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/README.md?plain=1#L273) mechanism allows for dynamic integration of custom passes into the compilation pipeline. A callback function, [`inspect_stages_hook`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/test/unit/plugins/custom_stages.py#L24), can modify the compilation stages, for example, by encapsulating logic to insert plugin passes into the [`pass_manager`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/ir.cc#L1832) using [`passes.plugin.add_plugin`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/README.md?plain=1#L135). This also supports arbitrary pass insertion by dynamically modifying the source code of Triton's [`make_ttir`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py#L211) or [`make_ttgir`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py#L228) methods using [`inspect.getsource`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/README.md?plain=1#L214), [`textwrap.dedent`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/README.md?plain=1#L214), and [`exec`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/include/Driver/Dispatch.h#L130). Furthermore, the entire compilation pipeline can be customized by capturing and overriding the source code of Triton's internal [`make_ttir`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py#L211) and [`make_ttgir`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/backend/compiler.py#L228) methods to dynamically load a new [`GPUOverrideBackend`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/README.md?plain=1#L274) class, replacing default stages with custom implementations.  
插件系统通过在运行时加载共享库来工作，这些库可以通过 `TRITON_PASS_PLUGIN_PATH` 环境变量指定。在 Python 中， `knobs.runtime.add_stages_inspection_hook` 机制允许将自定义插件动态集成到编译流程中。一个回调函数 `inspect_stages_hook` 可以修改编译阶段，例如通过封装逻辑将插件传递插入到 `pass_manager` 中，使用 `passes.plugin.add_plugin` 。这也支持通过使用 `inspect.getsource` 、 `textwrap.dedent` 和 `exec` 动态修改 Triton 的 `make_ttir` 或 `make_ttgir` 方法的源代码来插入任意传递。此外，整个编译流程可以通过捕获和覆盖 Triton 内部 `make_ttir` 和 `make_ttgir` 方法的源代码来定制，以动态加载一个新的 `GPUOverrideBackend` 类，用自定义实现替换默认阶段。

An example of a custom plugin, located in [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins), demonstrates the integration of a custom MLIR dialect named [`DialectPluginDialect`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/CMakeLists.txt#L7). This plugin defines custom operations and types and extends Triton's GPU-to-LLVM conversion process, translating these custom dialect operations and types into LLVM/NVVM. The dialect definition is handled by [`DialectPluginDialect`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/CMakeLists.txt#L7) within [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.h) and implemented in [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.cpp). Custom operations are defined in [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginOps.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginOps.h), and custom types are defined in [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginTypes.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginTypes.h). MLIR passes for this dialect are declared in [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.h), with their implementation in [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.cpp) providing the conversion logic. This includes the [`ConvertPluginGPUToLLVMPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.cpp#L79) which transforms custom GPU operations into LLVM representations, configurable by compute capability and PTX version. The plugin API functions, exposed via [`TRITON_PLUGIN_API`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/include/triton/Tools/PluginUtils.h#L16) in [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.cpp), allow external frameworks to dynamically add, register, enumerate, and query information about these custom passes and dialects.  
一个自定义插件的示例，位于 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins` ，展示了如何集成一个名为 `DialectPluginDialect` 的自定义 MLIR 方言。该插件定义了自定义操作和类型，并扩展了 Triton 的 GPU 到 LLVM 的转换过程，将这些自定义方言的操作和类型转换为 LLVM/NVVM。方言的定义由 `DialectPluginDialect` 在 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.h` 中处理，并在 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.cpp` 中实现。自定义操作定义在 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginOps.h` ，自定义类型定义在 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginTypes.h` 。该方言的 MLIR passes 在 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.h` 中声明，其实现位于 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.cpp` ，提供转换逻辑。这包括 `ConvertPluginGPUToLLVMPass` ，它将自定义 GPU 操作转换为 LLVM 表示形式，可通过计算能力和 PTX 版本进行配置。插件 API 函数，通过 `TRITON_PLUGIN_API` 在 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.cpp` 中暴露，允许外部框架动态添加、注册、枚举和查询关于这些自定义 passes 和方言的信息。

### Custom MLIR Dialect and Pass Development  
自定义 MLIR 方言和 Pass 开发

link

zoom\_in

The Triton compiler can be extended through a plugin system that allows the introduction of custom MLIR (Multi-Level Intermediate Representation) dialects, operations, types, and transformation passes. This extensibility facilitates out-of-tree customization of the Triton IR (TTIR) and Triton GPU IR (TTGIR) stages, enabling users to modify or introduce new compilation behaviors. A core example of this plugin mechanism is demonstrated in the [`DialectPlugin`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/include/triton/Tools/PluginUtils.h#L5), which showcases how to integrate a new dialect and its associated conversion logic into the Triton compilation pipeline.  
Triton 编译器可以通过插件系统进行扩展，该系统允许引入自定义的 MLIR（多层中间表示）方言、操作、类型和转换 passes。这种可扩展性促进了 Triton IR（TTIR）和 Triton GPU IR（TTGIR）阶段的树外定制，使用户能够修改或引入新的编译行为。这种插件机制的典型示例展示了 `DialectPlugin` ，它展示了如何将新的方言及其相关的转换逻辑集成到 Triton 编译流程中。

The process of creating a custom MLIR dialect within a Triton plugin involves several steps, orchestrated primarily through declarative specifications and CMake. First, the custom dialect itself, such as the [`DialectPluginDialect`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/CMakeLists.txt#L7) declared in [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.h), is defined. This declaration typically inherits from MLIR's [`Dialect`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/docs/conf.py#L62) class and can implement interfaces like [`BytecodeOpInterface`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.h#L4) for serialization support.  
在 Triton 插件中创建自定义 MLIR 方言的过程涉及多个步骤，主要通过声明式规范和 CMake 进行协调。首先，自定义方言本身，例如在 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.h` 中声明的 `DialectPluginDialect` ，需要被定义。这种声明通常继承自 MLIR 的 `Dialect` 类，并可以实现 `BytecodeOpInterface` 接口以支持序列化。

Custom operations and types belonging to this dialect are then defined. Operations, like those described in [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginOps.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginOps.h), leverage [`GET_OP_CLASSES`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Dialect/Triton/IR/Ops.cpp#L29) to generate their C++ definitions from declarative specifications. Similarly, custom types, declared in [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginTypes.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginTypes.h), use [`GET_TYPEDEF_CLASSES`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Dialect/Triton/IR/Types.cpp#L14) for their generation and registration. These generated components are then registered with the custom dialect during its initialization, as seen in the [`initialize`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/gluon/14-multicta.py#L702) method within [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.cpp).  
然后定义属于这个方言的自定义操作和类型。操作，如 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginOps.h` 中所述，利用 `GET_OP_CLASSES` 从声明性规范生成它们的 C++ 定义。类似地，在 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginTypes.h` 中声明的自定义类型使用 `GET_TYPEDEF_CLASSES` 进行生成和注册。这些生成的组件随后在自定义方言初始化期间进行注册，如在 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.cpp` 中的 `initialize` 方法中所示。

A critical aspect of integrating a custom dialect is defining the necessary transformation passes to convert its operations and types into lower-level MLIR dialects, such as LLVM/NVVM, which Triton can ultimately compile to machine code. The [`DialectPlugin`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/include/triton/Tools/PluginUtils.h#L5) includes passes like [`ConvertPluginGPUToLLVMPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.cpp#L79), which is declared in [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.h) and implemented in [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.cpp). This pass uses a [`PluginLLVMConversionTarget`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.cpp#L21) to specify which dialects are legal after conversion and which (like the custom [`DialectPluginDialect`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/CMakeLists.txt#L7)) must be converted. It also includes patterns, such as [`PluginMagicOpConversion`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.cpp#L36), to translate specific custom operations (e.g., [`MagicOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.cpp#L35)) into equivalent LLVM/NVVM operations, potentially utilizing GPU-specific intrinsics or operations. This conversion process integrates with Triton's existing infrastructure, including [`TritonGPUToLLVMTypeConverter`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/include/triton/Conversion/TritonGPUToLLVM/TypeConverter.h#L13) and [`mlir::triton::NVIDIA::TargetInfo`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.cpp#L89), allowing for target-specific code generation.  
将自定义方言集成的一个关键方面是定义必要的转换过程，以将其操作和类型转换为较低级别的 MLIR 方言，例如 LLVM/NVVM，Triton 最终可以将其编译为机器代码。 `DialectPlugin` 包括像 `ConvertPluginGPUToLLVMPass` 这样的过程，该过程在 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/include/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.h` 中声明并在 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginPasses.cpp` 中实现。此过程使用 `PluginLLVMConversionTarget` 来指定转换后哪些方言是合法的，哪些（如自定义的 `DialectPluginDialect` ）必须被转换。它还包括像 `PluginMagicOpConversion` 这样的模式，用于将特定的自定义操作（例如 `MagicOp` ）转换为等效的 LLVM/NVVM 操作，可能利用特定于 GPU 的内置函数或操作。此转换过程与 Triton 现有的基础设施集成，包括 `TritonGPUToLLVMTypeConverter` 和 `mlir::triton::NVIDIA::TargetInfo` ，允许进行针对特定目标的代码生成。

The plugin system also provides APIs for dynamic loading and management. Functions such as [`tritonAddPluginPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/TritonPlugin.cpp#L52), [`tritonRegisterPluginPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/TritonPlugin.cpp#L61), and [`tritonEnumeratePluginPasses`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/TritonPlugin.cpp#L70), exposed through [`TRITON_PLUGIN_API`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/include/triton/Tools/PluginUtils.h#L16) in [`examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.cpp), enable the Triton runtime to discover, register, and apply these custom passes. This dynamic loading capability allows for flexible extension of the compiler without recompiling the entire Triton project. For additional details on the overall plugin system, refer to [Compiler Extension and Plugin System](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#compiler-extension-and-plugin-system).  
插件系统还提供了用于动态加载和管理的 API。通过在 `examples/plugins/DialectPlugins/DialectPlugin/lib/DialectPlugin/DialectPluginDialect.cpp` 中通过 `TRITON_PLUGIN_API` 暴露的 `tritonAddPluginPass` 、 `tritonRegisterPluginPass` 和 `tritonEnumeratePluginPasses` 等函数，Triton 运行时能够发现、注册和应用这些自定义插件。这种动态加载功能允许在不重新编译整个 Triton 项目的情况下灵活扩展编译器。有关插件系统的更多详细信息，请参阅编译器扩展和插件系统。

## Performance Profiling and Debugging  
性能分析和调试

link

zoom\_in

Triton provides a comprehensive framework, Proton, for analyzing and optimizing the performance of Triton applications. This framework allows for detailed performance data collection, management of execution contexts, and analysis of collected metrics. It supports both NVIDIA and AMD GPUs, with capabilities for instruction sampling and intra-kernel instrumentation.  
Triton 提供了一个全面的框架 Proton，用于分析和优化 Triton 应用的性能。该框架支持详细的性能数据收集、执行上下文管理以及收集指标的分析。它支持 NVIDIA 和 AMD GPU，具备指令采样和内核内部仪器化功能。

The core of Proton's profiling capabilities is its session management, which allows users to start, activate, deactivate, and finalize profiling sessions. This lifecycle management is exposed through a Python API in [`third_party/proton/proton/profile.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/profile.py) and implemented in the C++ library exposed via [`third_party/proton/csrc/Proton.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/Proton.cpp). Proton also provides mechanisms to track execution contexts and operations through scopes and states, helping to delineate profiled regions of code. The [`scope`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/scope.py#L15) utility, defined in [`third_party/proton/proton/scope.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/scope.py), can mark specific code blocks for profiling, while [`state`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/test/unit/language/test_frontend.py#L162) in [`third_party/proton/proton/state.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/state.py) can annotate GPU operations with contextual information.  
Proton 的性能分析核心在于其会话管理，它允许用户启动、激活、停用和最终化性能分析会话。这种生命周期管理通过 `third_party/proton/proton/profile.py` 中的 Python API 暴露，并在通过 `third_party/proton/csrc/Proton.cpp` 暴露的 C++ 库中实现。Proton 还提供了通过作用域和状态追踪执行上下文和操作机制，帮助界定代码中被分析的区域。定义在 `third_party/proton/proton/scope.py` 中的 `scope` 工具可以标记特定代码块进行性能分析，而 `third_party/proton/proton/state.py` 中的 `state` 可以用上下文信息标注 GPU 操作。

Proton integrates with Triton's compilation pipeline through custom MLIR dialects. The Proton dialect, located in [`third_party/proton/Dialect`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect), includes [`ProtonDialect`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/Dialect/Proton/IR/Dialect.cpp#L27) and [`ProtonGPUDialect`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/Dialect/ProtonGPU/IR/Types.cpp#L18). These dialects enable program analysis by managing scope IDs for operations. They also define the intermediate representation for profiling-specific operations, which are then lowered through a multi-stage process. This lowering transforms high-level [`proton::RecordOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/triton_proton.cc#L81)s into GPU-specific profiling operations, including shared memory allocation and specialized instructions for NVIDIA and AMD targets. This process is managed by conversion passes such as [`ConvertProtonToProtonGPUPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonToProtonGPU/ProtonToProtonGPUPass.cpp#L171) in [`third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonToProtonGPU/ProtonToProtonGPUPass.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonToProtonGPU/ProtonToProtonGPUPass.cpp) and target-specific passes for LLVM conversion in [`third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM).  
Proton 通过自定义的 MLIR 语法与 Triton 的编译流程集成。Proton 语法位于 `third_party/proton/Dialect` ，包含 `ProtonDialect` 和 `ProtonGPUDialect` 。这些语法通过管理操作的作用域 ID 来实现程序分析，同时定义了针对性能分析操作的中间表示，这些操作随后通过多阶段流程进行转换。这种转换将高级 `proton::RecordOp` 转换为 GPU 特定的性能分析操作，包括共享内存分配和针对 NVIDIA 与 AMD 目标的专用指令。这一过程由 `ConvertProtonToProtonGPUPass` 在 `third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonToProtonGPU/ProtonToProtonGPUPass.cpp` 中的转换阶段以及 `third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM` 中 LLVM 转换的特定目标阶段管理。

For data collection and analysis, Proton employs a framework for processing binary trace data. This framework, found in [`third_party/proton/common`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common), handles circular buffer layouts and can output data in formats compatible with tools like Chrome Trace. The [`ByteSpan`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/ByteSpan.h#L16) class in [`third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/ByteSpan.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/ByteSpan.h) provides safe, sequential reading from byte buffers, while [`CircularLayoutParser`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/CircularLayoutParser.h#L55) in [`third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/CircularLayoutParser.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/CircularLayoutParser.h) specializes in parsing trace data from circular buffer layouts. A [`StreamChromeTraceWriter`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/TraceWriter.h#L45) in [`third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/TraceWriter.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/TraceWriter.h) generates Chrome Trace Format output for visualization.  
为数据收集和分析，Proton 采用一个处理二进制跟踪数据的框架。该框架位于 `third_party/proton/common` ，能够处理循环缓冲区布局，并可以输出与 Chrome Trace 等工具兼容的数据格式。 `third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/ByteSpan.h` 中的 `ByteSpan` 类提供从字节数据缓冲区安全、顺序的读取，而 `third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/CircularLayoutParser.h` 中的 `CircularLayoutParser` 专门用于解析循环缓冲区布局中的跟踪数据。 `third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/TraceWriter.h` 中的 `StreamChromeTraceWriter` 生成 Chrome Trace 格式输出，用于可视化。

Proton also supports various profiling backends. For NVIDIA GPUs, it uses [`cupti`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Driver/GPU/CuptiApi.cpp#L7) for default profiling and instruction sampling. For AMD GPUs, it uses [`roctracer`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/include/Driver/GPU/RoctracerApi.h#L9). Additionally, an [`instrumentation`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/hooks/instrumentation.py#L48) backend is available for both architectures, allowing for custom metrics and advanced intra-kernel profiling. These backends are managed by components within [`third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Profiler`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Profiler). The framework also includes a command-line utility, [`proton`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/knobs.py#L570), in [`third_party/proton/proton/proton.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/proton.py) for profiling Python scripts and [`pytest`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/Makefile#L9) tests, and a [`proton-viewer`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/setup.py#L512) in [`third_party/proton/proton/viewer.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/viewer.py) for visualizing and analyzing profiling data using [`hatchet`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/docs/requirements.txt#L11).  
Proton 还支持多种分析后端。对于 NVIDIA GPU，它使用 `cupti` 进行默认分析和指令采样。对于 AMD GPU，它使用 `roctracer` 。此外，两种架构都可用 `instrumentation` 后端，允许自定义指标和高级内核内分析。这些后端由 `third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Profiler` 内部组件管理。该框架还包括 `third_party/proton/proton/proton.py` 中的命令行工具 `proton` ，用于分析 Python 脚本和 `pytest` 测试，以及 `third_party/proton/proton/viewer.py` 中的 `proton-viewer` ，用于使用 `hatchet` 可视化和分析分析数据。

Debugging in Triton is aided by features such as interpreted execution. While the current documentation primarily focuses on performance profiling, the ability to trace and instrument code at various levels of the compilation pipeline, from Python AST to MLIR dialects, inherently supports identifying and diagnosing issues. For examples of how these profiling capabilities are utilized, particularly for intra-kernel analysis, refer to the [Intra-Kernel Profiling and Instrumentation](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#performance-profiling-and-debugging-intra-kernel-profiling-and-instrumentation) section and the tutorials in [`third_party/proton/tutorials`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/tutorials).  
Triton 中的调试功能受益于解释执行等特性。虽然当前文档主要关注性能分析，但能够在编译管道的各个级别（从 Python AST 到 MLIR 方言）跟踪和插入代码的能力，本质上支持识别和诊断问题。有关这些分析功能如何使用的示例，特别是用于内核内分析的，请参阅内核内分析和插入部分以及 `third_party/proton/tutorials` 中的教程。

### Proton Profiling Framework Overview  
Proton Profiling Framework 概述

link

zoom\_in

Proton is a profiling framework designed for Triton applications to collect and analyze performance data with low overhead. It is structured with a Python API that interacts with an underlying C++ library, providing session management, context tracking, and metric recording. The framework supports profiling on both NVIDIA and AMD GPUs.  
Proton 是一个为 Triton 应用设计的性能分析框架，用于以低开销收集和分析性能数据。它采用 Python API 与底层的 C++库交互，提供会话管理、上下文跟踪和指标记录功能。该框架支持在 NVIDIA 和 AMD GPU 上进行性能分析。

The core of Proton's functionality is exposed through the Python API, particularly via [`third_party/proton/proton/__init__.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/__init__.py). This interface allows users to initiate, control, and finalize profiling sessions. Functions such as [`start`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/profile.py#L57), [`activate`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/profile.py#L135), [`deactivate`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/profile.py#L157), and [`finalize`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/profile.py#L180) manage the lifecycle of a profiling session, while decorators like [`profile`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/profile.py#L233) simplify the instrumentation of Python functions. Context management is handled by [`scope`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/scope.py#L15) and [`state`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/test/unit/language/test_frontend.py#L162) utilities, defined in [`third_party/proton/proton/scope.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/scope.py) and [`third_party/proton/proton/state.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/state.py) respectively, which delineate profiling regions and mark execution states. These Python-level operations interact with the C++ backend through [`pybind11`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/setup.py#L23) bindings, as defined in [`third_party/proton/csrc/Proton.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/Proton.cpp).  
Proton 的核心功能通过 Python API 暴露，特别是通过 `third_party/proton/proton/__init__.py` 。这个接口允许用户启动、控制和结束分析会话。 `start` 、 `activate` 、 `deactivate` 和 `finalize` 等函数管理分析会话的生命周期，而 `profile` 等装饰器简化了 Python 函数的插桩。上下文管理由 `scope` 和 `state` 工具处理，分别定义在 `third_party/proton/proton/scope.py` 和 `third_party/proton/proton/state.py` 中，它们界定分析区域并标记执行状态。这些 Python 级别的操作通过 `pybind11` 绑定与 C++后端交互，如 `third_party/proton/csrc/Proton.cpp` 中定义的那样。

The C++ library, built from the sources in [`third_party/proton/csrc`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc), is responsible for the actual performance data collection and management. It provides mechanisms for tracking execution scopes and operations ([`record_scope`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/scope.py#L46), [`enter_op`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/README.md?plain=1#L302)), managing profiling states ([`enter_state`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/state.py#L64), [`exit_state`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/state.py#L68)), and recording various scalar and tensor metrics ([`add_metrics`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/scope.py#L50)). This layer includes abstractions for GPU drivers (CUDA and HIP) and integrates with profiling APIs like CUPTI for NVIDIA and ROCtracer for AMD. The [`SessionManager`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/include/Session/Session.h#L73) in [`third_party/proton/csrc/include/Session`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/include/Session) orchestrates multiple profiling sessions, ensuring proper data dispatch and retrieval.  
这个 C++库，由 `third_party/proton/csrc` 中的源代码构建，负责实际性能数据的收集和管理。它提供了跟踪执行范围和操作（ `record_scope` ， `enter_op` ）、管理分析状态（ `enter_state` ， `exit_state` ）以及记录各种标量和张量指标（ `add_metrics` ）的机制。这一层包括对 GPU 驱动（CUDA 和 HIP）的抽象，并与 NVIDIA 的 CUPTI 和 AMD 的 ROCtracer 等分析 API 集成。 `SessionManager` 在 `third_party/proton/csrc/include/Session` 中协调多个分析会话，确保数据的正确发送和检索。

Proton also includes an MLIR-based profiling dialect. This dialect, detailed further in [MLIR-Based Profiling Dialects and Lowering](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#performance-profiling-and-debugging-mlir-based-profiling-dialects-and-lowering), allows for instrumentation directly within the Triton compiler's intermediate representation. It defines [`Proton`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/CMakeLists.txt#L21) and [`ProtonGPU`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L11) MLIR dialects, which enable a multi-stage lowering process to generate GPU-specific code for profiling. This approach ensures fine-grained control over instrumentation and optimized performance data collection on the hardware.  
Proton 还包含一个基于 MLIR 的分析方言。这个方言在《基于 MLIR 的分析方言和降级》中有详细说明，允许直接在 Triton 编译器的中间表示中进行仪器化。它定义了 `Proton` 和 `ProtonGPU` MLIR 方言，这些方言支持多阶段降级过程，以生成用于分析的 GPU 特定代码。这种方法确保了对仪器化的细粒度控制，并在硬件上优化性能数据的收集。

The collected profiling data can be retrieved and managed through functions like [`get_data`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/data.py#L20) and [`get_data_msgpack`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/data.py#L37), which provide access to raw profiling data in various formats. The framework also supports analyzing this data for insights into application performance. For more details on these functionalities, refer to [Data Collection, Storage, and Analysis](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#performance-profiling-and-debugging-data-collection-storage-and-analysis).  
收集到的分析数据可以通过 `get_data` 和 `get_data_msgpack` 等函数进行检索和管理，这些函数提供对各种格式的原始分析数据的访问。该框架还支持分析这些数据以获取应用程序性能的洞察。有关这些功能的更多详细信息，请参阅《数据收集、存储和分析》。

### Intra-Kernel Profiling and Instrumentation  
内核内部剖析与插装

link

python

content\_copyCopy  复制

\# Enable Triton semantic for profiling. \# Triton's IR undergoes aggressive compiler rewrites, which can affect \# instrumentation. Use with caution. pl.enable\_semantic("triton") @triton.jit def blocked\_matmul\_pipelined\_kernel(...): \# Stubbed for brevity \# Mark the entry of the kernel scope for profiling. pl.enter\_scope("blocked\_matmul\_pipelined\_kernel") \# ... (kernel logic) ... \# Use 'with pl.scope()' for convenient entry/exit of profiling regions. with pl.scope("tma\_loads\_issue"): \# Asynchronous TMA loads for matrix A and B. tma.async\_copy\_global\_to\_shared(...) \# Stubbed with pl.scope("tma\_loads\_wait"): \# Wait for TMA loads to complete. mbarrier.wait(...) \# Stubbed \# Another profiling scope for the Warp-Group Matrix Multiply Accumulate (WGMMA) wait. with pl.scope("wgmma\_wait"): acc = warpgroup\_mma\_wait(...) \# Stubbed \# Mark the exit of the kernel scope. pl.exit\_scope("blocked\_matmul\_pipelined\_kernel")  
\# 启用 Triton 语义进行性能分析。 # Triton 的中间表示会经历激进的编译器重写，这可能会影响 # 仪器化。请谨慎使用。 pl.enable\_semantic("triton") @triton.jit def blocked\_matmul\_pipelined\_kernel(...): # 为简洁起见，此处为占位符 # 标记内核作用域的入口，用于分析。 pl.enter\_scope("blocked\_matmul\_pipelined\_kernel") # ... (内核逻辑) ... # 使用 'with pl.scope()' 方便地进入/退出分析区域。 with pl.scope("tma\_loads\_issue"): # 矩阵 A 和 B 的异步 TMA 加载数据。 tma.async\_copy\_global\_to\_shared(...) # Stubbed with pl.scope("tma\_loads\_wait"): # 等待 TMA 加载完成。 mbarrier.wait(...) # Stubbed # 另一个用于 Warp-Group 矩阵乘累加（WGMMA）等待的剖析范围。 with pl.scope("wgmma\_wait"): acc = warpgroup\_mma\_wait(...) # 占位符 # 标记内核作用域的退出。 pl.exit\_scope("blocked\_matmul\_pipelined\_kernel")

Triton provides advanced techniques for profiling the performance of GPU kernels at a fine-grained level, enabling analysis of execution within specific code regions and the collection of cycle counts. This intra-kernel profiling capability is primarily supported through two approaches: the TTGIR override method and the Proton DSL method.  
Triton 提供了在细粒度级别上分析 GPU 内核性能的高级技术，能够分析特定代码区域的执行情况并收集周期计数。这种内核内部分析能力主要通过两种方法实现：TTGIR 覆盖方法以及 Proton DSL 方法。

The **TTGIR override approach** facilitates profiling existing Triton DSL kernels without direct modifications to their source code. This method involves generating Triton Generated Intermediate Representation (TTGIR) files, which are then instrumented by injecting [`proton.record`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/Proton/ops.mlir#L6) operations. Execution of the kernel is then configured to use these modified TTGIR files, allowing for the collection of profiling data. This workflow is demonstrated through examples like [`add_kernel`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/01-vector-add.py#L30) in [`third_party/proton/tutorials/intra_kernel/example_override.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/tutorials/intra_kernel/example_override.py), where external scripts handle the generation and modification of TTGIR.  
TTGIR 覆盖方法能够在不直接修改其源代码的情况下，对现有的 Triton DSL 内核进行性能分析。该方法涉及生成 Triton 生成中间表示（TTGIR）文件，然后通过注入 `proton.record` 操作来对这些文件进行插桩。随后配置内核执行使用这些修改后的 TTGIR 文件，从而收集性能分析数据。这一工作流程通过 `add_kernel` 中的 `third_party/proton/tutorials/intra_kernel/example_override.py` 等示例进行演示，其中外部脚本负责处理 TTGIR 的生成和修改。

The **Proton DSL approach** integrates profiling directly into Triton and Gluon DSL kernels. This method uses [`pl.enter_scope`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/README.md?plain=1#L161) and [`pl.scope`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/README.md?plain=1#L165) constructs to explicitly mark regions within a kernel for profiling. This allows developers to analyze performance within specific sections of their code, such as asynchronous memory operations or matrix multiplication stages, as seen in the [`blocked_matmul_pipelined_kernel`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/gluon/05-wgmma.py#L526) example for NVIDIA Hopper GPUs in [`third_party/proton/tutorials/intra_kernel/example_dsl.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/tutorials/intra_kernel/example_dsl.py). The [`pl.enable_semantic`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/README.md?plain=1#L151) function explicitly activates Proton DSL for Triton kernels, ensuring that these profiling directives are recognized.  
Proton DSL 方法将性能分析直接集成到 Triton 和 Gluon DSL 内核中。该方法使用 `pl.enter_scope` 和 `pl.scope` 结构来明确标记内核中的性能分析区域。这使得开发者能够分析代码特定部分的性能，例如异步内存操作或矩阵乘法阶段，正如在 `blocked_matmul_pipelined_kernel` 中为 NVIDIA Hopper GPU 提供的 `third_party/proton/tutorials/intra_kernel/example_dsl.py` 示例所示。 `pl.enable_semantic` 函数明确激活 Proton DSL，确保这些性能分析指令被识别。

Both approaches leverage the Proton profiling framework, which manages the lifecycle of profiling data collection. The [`proton.start`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/knobs.py#L551) function initializes a profiling session, specifying the backend (e.g., [`"instrumentation"`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/hooks/instrumentation.py#L48)) and data collection type (e.g., [`"trace"`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Data/TraceData.cpp#L59) for timeline traces or [`"op-measure"`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/tutorials/intra_kernel/README.md?plain=1#L54) for operation-level metrics). After kernel execution, [`proton.finalize`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/09-persistent-matmul.py#L757) concludes the session and writes the collected data to output files. These output formats include [`.chrome_trace`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/.gitignore#L6) files for timeline visualizations and [`.hatchet`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/tutorials/09-persistent-matmul.py#L726) files for scope-level performance metrics, providing insights into [`normalized_cycles`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/include/Data/Metric.h#L372) and total [`cycles`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/triton/knobs.py#L157). The [`InstrumentationHook`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/hooks/instrumentation.py#L131) in [`third_party/proton/proton/hooks/instrumentation.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/hooks/instrumentation.py) plays a crucial role in injecting Proton-related passes into Triton's compilation pipeline, overriding allocators, and managing the collection and processing of profiling data from the GPU device. Further details on the Proton framework can be found in [Proton Profiling Framework Overview](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#performance-profiling-and-debugging-proton-profiling-framework-overview).  
两种方法都利用了 Proton 分析框架，该框架管理分析数据收集的生命周期。 `proton.start` 函数初始化分析会话，指定后端（例如 `"instrumentation"` ）和数据收集类型（例如 `"trace"` 用于时间线跟踪或 `"op-measure"` 用于操作级指标）。内核执行后， `proton.finalize` 结束会话并将收集的数据写入输出文件。这些输出格式包括 `.chrome_trace` 文件用于时间线可视化，以及 `.hatchet` 文件用于作用域级性能指标，提供对 `normalized_cycles` 和总 `cycles` 的洞察。 `InstrumentationHook` 在 `third_party/proton/proton/hooks/instrumentation.py` 中起着关键作用，用于将 Proton 相关 passes 注入 Triton 的编译流程，覆盖分配器，并管理从 GPU 设备收集和处理分析数据。有关 Proton 框架的更多详细信息，请参阅 Proton 分析框架概述。

Profiling accuracy and data collection can be configured through various options, including [`clock32`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/mode.py#L40) for low-overhead 32-bit clock recording, [`time_shift`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/mode.py#L37) to deduct constant profiling overhead, [`sched_stores`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/mode.py#L38) for cycle-accurate operation latency, and [`sched_barriers`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/mode.py#L39) to constrain instruction scheduling on AMD GPUs. Buffer configurations, such as [`buffer_type`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/mode.py#L80) ([`shared`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/unittest/Dialect/TritonGPU/DumpLayoutTest.cpp#L25) or [`global`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/test/unit/runtime/test_cache.py#L287)) and [`buffer_size`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/mode.py#L81), control where and how profiling data is stored per thread block. Additionally, [`warp sampling`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/README.md?plain=1#L103) ([`sampling_strategy`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/mode.py#L76) and [`sampling_options`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/mode.py#L77)) enables focused profiling on specific warps, allowing for more granular event capture within a given buffer size. These options are detailed in [`third_party/proton/tutorials/intra_kernel/README.md`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/tutorials/intra_kernel/README.md).  
性能分析准确性和数据收集可以通过多种选项进行配置，包括 `clock32` 用于低开销的 32 位时钟记录、 `time_shift` 用于扣除常量性能分析开销、 `sched_stores` 用于精确到周期的操作延迟，以及 `sched_barriers` 用于在 AMD GPU 上限制指令调度。缓冲区配置，如 `buffer_type` （ `shared` 或 `global` ）和 `buffer_size` ，控制每个线程块中性能分析数据存储的位置和方式。此外， `warp sampling` （ `sampling_strategy` 和 `sampling_options` ）启用对特定 warp 的聚焦性能分析，允许在给定的缓冲区大小内进行更细粒度的事件捕获。这些选项在 `third_party/proton/tutorials/intra_kernel/README.md` 中有详细说明。

### MLIR-Based Profiling Dialects and Lowering  
基于 MLIR 的分析方言和降级

link

zoom\_in

Profiling in Triton is integrated into the MLIR pipeline through the Proton and ProtonGPU dialects, enabling instrumentation and performance data collection during GPU kernel execution. This framework captures metrics like cycle counts from high-level [`proton::RecordOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/triton_proton.cc#L81) operations and lowers them to GPU-specific instructions for NVIDIA and AMD targets, including shared memory allocation and buffer management.  
Triton 中的性能分析通过 Proton 和 ProtonGPU 方言集成到 MLIR 流程中，能够在 GPU 内核执行期间进行代码插装和性能数据收集。该框架捕获来自高级 `proton::RecordOp` 操作的指标（如周期计数），并将其转换为针对 NVIDIA 和 AMD 目标的特定 GPU 指令，包括共享内存分配和缓冲区管理。

The process begins with the [`ProtonDialect`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/Dialect/Proton/IR/Dialect.cpp#L27) (defined in [`third_party/proton/Dialect/include/Dialect/Proton/IR/Dialect.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/include/Dialect/Proton/IR/Dialect.h)), which introduces the [`proton::RecordOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/triton_proton.cc#L81). This operation marks points in the program for profiling, indicating either the start or end of a region. A static analysis phase, [`ScopeIdAllocation`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/include/Analysis/ScopeIdAllocation.h#L17) (implemented in [`third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/Analysis/ScopeIdAllocation.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/Analysis/ScopeIdAllocation.cpp)), identifies [`proton::RecordOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/triton_proton.cc#L81) pairs, assigns unique scope identifiers, and infers parent-child relationships between scopes within a function. This analysis is extended across the entire module by [`ModuleScopeIdAllocation`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/include/Analysis/ScopeIdAllocation.h#L62) to ensure global uniqueness and maintain hierarchical relationships.  
该过程始于 `ProtonDialect` （定义于 `third_party/proton/Dialect/include/Dialect/Proton/IR/Dialect.h` ），它引入了 `proton::RecordOp` 。此操作在程序中标记用于分析的位置，表示某个区域的开始或结束。静态分析阶段 `ScopeIdAllocation` （实现于 `third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/Analysis/ScopeIdAllocation.cpp` ）识别 `proton::RecordOp` 对，分配唯一的范围标识符，并推断函数内作用域之间的父子关系。通过 `ModuleScopeIdAllocation` 将此分析扩展到整个模块，以确保全局唯一性并保持层级关系。

Following this analysis, the [`ConvertProtonToProtonGPUPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonToProtonGPU/ProtonToProtonGPUPass.cpp#L171) (implemented in [`third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonToProtonGPU/ProtonToProtonGPUPass.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonToProtonGPU/ProtonToProtonGPUPass.cpp)) transforms [`proton::RecordOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/triton_proton.cc#L81) instances into [`ProtonGPU`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L11) dialect operations, specialized for GPU execution. This pass configures how profiling data is collected and managed on the GPU, allowing customization of metrics, sampling strategies, and buffer types (shared or global memory). For instance, it implements a circular buffer profiling mechanism by calculating memory allocations, creating global scratch memory, and allocating profiling buffers. It also initializes the profiling system and modifies [`triton::gpu::WarpSpecializeOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/lib/Dialect/TritonNvidiaGPU/IR/Ops.cpp#L183) operations to pass profiling buffers, ensuring that [`proton::RecordOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/triton_proton.cc#L81)s are replaced with [`gpu::ReadCounterOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonToProtonGPU/ProtonToProtonGPUPass.cpp#L104) and [`gpu::CircularStoreOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonToProtonGPU/ProtonToProtonGPUPass.cpp#L107) to store collected data.  
根据这项分析， `ConvertProtonToProtonGPUPass` （在 `third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonToProtonGPU/ProtonToProtonGPUPass.cpp` 中实现）将 `proton::RecordOp` 实例转换为 `ProtonGPU` 方言操作，这些操作专门针对 GPU 执行。此转换配置了在 GPU 上收集和管理分析数据的方式，允许自定义指标、采样策略和缓冲区类型（共享或全局内存）。例如，它通过计算内存分配、创建全局临时内存以及分配分析缓冲区来实现循环缓冲区分析机制。它还初始化了分析系统，并修改了 `triton::gpu::WarpSpecializeOp` 操作以传递分析缓冲区，确保 `proton::RecordOp` 被替换为 `gpu::ReadCounterOp` 和 `gpu::CircularStoreOp` 以存储收集的数据。

The final stage involves converting the [`ProtonGPU`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L11) dialect operations into LLVM IR, which is handled by dedicated passes for NVIDIA and AMD GPUs. The [`ProtonGPUToLLVM`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L6) conversion ([`third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/PatternProtonGPUOpToLLVM.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/PatternProtonGPUOpToLLVM.cpp)) converts operations such as [`ReadCounterOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonToProtonGPU/ProtonToProtonGPUPass.cpp#L104) to hardware clock reads and [`CircularStoreOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/Dialect/ProtonGPU/IR/Ops.cpp#L22) to buffer write operations.  
最终阶段涉及将 `ProtonGPU` 方言操作转换为 LLVM IR，这由针对 NVIDIA 和 AMD GPU 的专用传递处理。 `ProtonGPUToLLVM` 转换（ `third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/PatternProtonGPUOpToLLVM.cpp` ）将 `ReadCounterOp` 等操作转换为硬件时钟读取，将 `CircularStoreOp` 转换为缓冲区写入操作。

For NVIDIA GPUs, the [`ConvertProtonNvidiaGPUToLLVM`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/ProtonNvidiaGPUToLLVM/ConvertProtonGPUToLLVM.cpp#L45) pass (in [`third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/ProtonNvidiaGPUToLLVM/ConvertProtonGPUToLLVM.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/ProtonNvidiaGPUToLLVM/ConvertProtonGPUToLLVM.cpp)) converts [`ProtonGPU`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/bin/RegisterTritonDialects.h#L11) operations to LLVM and NVVM dialects. It includes NVIDIA-specific patterns for operations like [`CircularStoreOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/Dialect/ProtonGPU/IR/Ops.cpp#L22) that generate [`st.global.cg`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/test/unit/language/test_core.py#L4456) PTX instructions for global memory and delegate to shared memory operations. NVIDIA-specific [`TargetInfo`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUToLLVM/TargetInfo.h#L10) implementations provide hardware details such as clock counters and SM IDs.  
对于 NVIDIA GPU， `ConvertProtonNvidiaGPUToLLVM` pass（在 `third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/ProtonNvidiaGPUToLLVM/ConvertProtonGPUToLLVM.cpp` 中）将 `ProtonGPU` 操作转换为 LLVM 和 NVVM 语法。它包括针对 `CircularStoreOp` 等操作的 NVIDIA 特定模式，这些操作为全局内存生成 `st.global.cg` PTX 指令，并将任务委托给共享内存操作。NVIDIA 特定的 `TargetInfo` 实现提供了硬件细节，例如时钟计数器和 SM ID。

For AMD GPUs, the [`ConvertProtonAMDGPUToLLVM`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/ProtonAMDGPUToLLVM/ConvertProtonGPUToLLVM.cpp#L45) pass (in [`third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/ProtonAMDGPUToLLVM/ConvertProtonGPUToLLVM.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/ProtonAMDGPUToLLVM/ConvertProtonGPUToLLVM.cpp)) performs a similar conversion to LLVM and ROCDL dialects. AMD-specific patterns for [`CircularStoreOp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/Dialect/ProtonGPU/IR/Ops.cpp#L22) use [`mlir::LLVM::AMD::llStore`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUToLLVM/TargetInfo.cpp#L153) for global memory. Additionally, the [`AddSchedBarriers`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/ProtonAMDGPUToLLVM/AddSchedBarriers.cpp#L23) pass inserts [`ROCDL::SchedBarrier`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/python/src/gluon_ir.cc#L1088) around profiling operations to ensure correct hardware scheduling on AMD GPUs. AMD-specific [`TargetInfo`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/amd/lib/TritonAMDGPUToLLVM/TargetInfo.h#L10) implementations provide functions for accessing [`llvm.amdgcn.s.memtime`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/Proton/amd/protongpu_to_llvm.mlir#L23) and [`llvm.amdgcn.s.memrealtime`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/test/Proton/amd/protongpu_to_llvm.mlir#L97), and computing a unique global compute unit ID.  
对于 AMD GPU， `ConvertProtonAMDGPUToLLVM` pass（在 `third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/ProtonAMDGPUToLLVM/ConvertProtonGPUToLLVM.cpp` 中）执行与 LLVM 和 ROCDL 方言类似的转换。AMD 特定的 `CircularStoreOp` 模式使用 `mlir::LLVM::AMD::llStore` 用于全局内存。此外， `AddSchedBarriers` pass 在性能分析操作周围插入 `ROCDL::SchedBarrier` ，以确保在 AMD GPU 上正确的硬件调度。AMD 特定的 `TargetInfo` 实现提供用于访问 `llvm.amdgcn.s.memtime` 和 `llvm.amdgcn.s.memrealtime` 的函数，并计算唯一的全局计算单元 ID。

The [`AllocateProtonSharedMemoryPass`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/AllocateProtonSharedMemory.cpp#L13) (in [`third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/AllocateProtonSharedMemory.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/AllocateProtonSharedMemory.cpp)) is responsible for allocating shared memory for profiling buffers, ensuring proper alignment and avoiding conflicts with other shared memory allocations. This multi-stage lowering process allows for fine-grained control over profiling while adapting to specific GPU architectures.  
`AllocateProtonSharedMemoryPass` （在 `third_party/proton/Dialect/lib/ProtonGPUToLLVM/AllocateProtonSharedMemory.cpp` 中）负责为分析缓冲区分配共享内存，确保正确的对齐并避免与其他共享内存分配冲突。这种多阶段优化过程允许在适应特定 GPU 架构的同时，对分析进行细粒度控制。

### Data Collection, Storage, and Analysis  
数据收集、存储和分析

link

zoom\_in

The Proton profiling framework collects raw profiling data from GPU devices and processes it into various formats for analysis. The core data management is handled by the [`Data`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/include/Data/Data.h#L79) class in [`third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Data/Data.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Data/Data.cpp), which supports different metric types and organizes them across profiling phases. This class offers methods to add operational metrics, manage profiling phases, and serialize collected data.  
Proton 分析框架从 GPU 设备收集原始分析数据，并将其处理成多种格式以供分析。核心数据管理由 `Data` 中的 `third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Data/Data.cpp` 类负责，该类支持不同指标类型，并在分析阶段中组织它们。此类提供添加操作指标、管理分析阶段以及序列化收集数据的方法。

Raw data collection on the GPU side, especially for performance traces, involves circular buffer layouts.
