The [`CircularLayoutParser`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/CircularLayoutParser.h#L55) in [`third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/CircularLayoutParser.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/CircularLayoutParser.h) is designed to parse this type of data, extracting metadata and profile events. This parser can reconstruct event timelines even from malformed sequences and adjust cycle timings. The process of translating raw bytes into structured entries is facilitated by the [`EntryDecoder`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/EntryDecoder.h#L17), as detailed in [`third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/EntryDecoder.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/EntryDecoder.h), which handles various integer types and specific cycle entries.  
GPU 侧的原始数据收集，尤其是性能跟踪，涉及循环缓冲区布局。 `CircularLayoutParser` 在 `third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/CircularLayoutParser.h` 中设计用于解析此类数据，提取元数据和跟踪事件。该解析器可以从损坏的序列中重建事件时间线，并调整周期时间。将原始字节转换为结构化条目的过程由 `EntryDecoder` 促进，如 `third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/EntryDecoder.h` 中详细所述，它处理各种整数类型和特定周期条目。

Once collected and parsed, the profiling data can be stored and analyzed using different output formats. The [`TraceData`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/include/Data/TraceData.h#L10) class in [`third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Data/TraceData.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Data/TraceData.cpp) manages hierarchical tracing information, including execution contexts and events, and provides functionality to serialize this data. For instance, the [`StreamChromeTraceWriter`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/TraceWriter.h#L45) in [`third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/TraceWriter.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/TraceWriter.h) converts internal [`KernelTrace`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Data/TraceData.cpp#L220) data into the Chrome Trace Format, which is suitable for visualization in [`chrome://tracing`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/README.md?plain=1#L274).  
一旦收集并解析，分析数据可以采用不同的输出格式进行存储和分析。在 `third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Data/TraceData.cpp` 中的 `TraceData` 类管理层次化跟踪信息，包括执行上下文和事件，并提供序列化这些数据的功能。例如，在 `third_party/proton/common/include/TraceDataIO/TraceWriter.h` 中的 `StreamChromeTraceWriter` 将内部 `KernelTrace` 数据转换为 Chrome Trace Format，这种格式适合在 `chrome://tracing` 中进行可视化。

For more in-depth analysis, especially for hierarchical performance data, the system also supports serialization to the Hatchet format, which is processed by the Python-based viewer in [`third_party/proton/proton/viewer.py`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/proton/viewer.py). This viewer leverages the [`hatchet`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/docs/requirements.txt#L11) library to manipulate tree-based performance data, allowing for filtering, metric derivation (like device utilization or flop/byte rates), and hierarchical display of performance trees or sorted lists. The [`TreeData`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/include/Data/TreeData.h#L16) class in [`third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Data/TreeData.cpp`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Data/TreeData.cpp) is responsible for managing this tree-structured profiling data, capturing execution contexts and associated metrics, and serializing it into Hatchet-compatible JSON or MessagePack formats.  
为了进行更深入的分析，特别是针对层次化的性能数据，系统还支持序列化为 Hatchet 格式，该格式由基于 Python 的查看器 `third_party/proton/proton/viewer.py` 处理。该查看器利用 `hatchet` 库来操作基于树的性能数据，允许进行过滤、指标推导（如设备利用率或 flop/byte 率），以及性能树或排序列表的层次化显示。 `third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Data/TreeData.cpp` 中的 `TreeData` 类负责管理这种树结构的分析数据，捕获执行上下文和关联指标，并将其序列化为与 Hatchet 兼容的 JSON 或 MessagePack 格式。

Utilities for device management, such as [`Device.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/csrc/lib/Data/TreeData.cpp#L4) in [`third_party/proton/common/include/Device.h`](https://github.com/triton-lang/triton/blob/ec77306bca6d4a4b157e979a363df7fe610e0363/third_party/proton/common/include/Device.h), provide abstractions for querying GPU properties, which are then incorporated into the profiling data for device-specific analysis. Further details on the Python API for managing profiling sessions and performance data collection can be found in [Proton Profiling Framework Overview](https://codewiki.google/github.com/triton-lang/triton#performance-profiling-and-debugging-proton-profiling-framework-overview).  
用于设备管理的工具，如 `Device.h` 中的 `third_party/proton/common/include/Device.h` ，提供了查询 GPU 属性的上层抽象，这些属性随后被整合到用于设备特定分析的剖析数据中。有关管理剖析会话和性能数据收集的 Python API 的更多详细信息，请参阅 Proton Profiling Framework Overview。
